Current Affairs Commentary

A Further Experiment in Mass Education

— Like

Adult education began with the arrival of this century. It initially did not have a definite position in the educational systems of various countries. However, with the government's close attention, it has gradually become an important part of national education. For example, Italy unified public and private mass schools under the so-called "Committee Against Illiteracy" (Comitato Contro Analfabet＇smo) and unified social education programs under the "National After-Work Activities Headquarters" (Opera Nazionale Ddopolavoro). This firmly demonstrates the government's determination and courage in vigorously implementing mass education. Furthermore, the governments of various German states subsidize "People's High Schools" (Volksbochschule) as stipulated in the federal constitution. The "University Tutorial Classes," initially organized by the Labor Education Association in England, are also subject to regulations formulated by the Ministry of Education and receive subsidies from the central and local governments according to law. These are all the most notable proofs. Whether it is in the competition of national intelligence or in the support of democratic forces, mass education has an urgent need.

China's mass education movement began with the establishment of the Chinese National Association of the Mass Education Movement in the twelfth year of the Republic. It saw a tremendous advance with the success of the National Revolution in the sixteenth year of the Republic. In recent years, various local mass education, rural construction, and rural service experimental institutions have gradually attracted the attention of the general public. Recently, the Jiangsu Provincial Education College held its seventh anniversary celebration and exhibition of achievements. The Minister of Education and the director of the relevant department personally came to inspect. Minister Wang said in his speech at the college, "I hope that all teachers and students will, with a full spirit of service, strive to establish the academic field of mass education, making mass education scientific rather than just common sense." This also demonstrates the government's attention to mass education. Originally, all academic fields originate from real-life activities. Starting from practical activities, exploring their principles, and standardizing their methods, they become academic fields. And academic fields, in turn, guide practical activities. There is no need to waste words or research on why mass education must be promoted. Only how to promote it effectively is what needs to be explored by various local experimental and research institutions in their actual activities to find the correct principles and methods. If with certain funds and talents, certain undertakings are operated, and the result is only equal to undertakings that anyone can hold with this funding and talents, then why should these experimental and research institutions be established? Therefore, whether this type of institution can fulfill its mission depends on whether it can provide correct and effective principles and methods in education. The rationale is clear. Therefore, I feel that Minister Wang's saying "making mass education scientific rather than just common sense" contains a great truth and has much in common.

Furthermore, since the Ministry of Education's first Mass Education Committee meeting in the twenty-third year of the Republic resolved on "the implementation pathways of mass education" and instructed that "various mass education institutions should provide practical life organizations, tools, and technologies, and do their best to organize experimental zones and other experimental undertakings," the scope of so-called mass education has expanded and is no longer limited to literacy education. Currently, larger mass education experimental zones mostly include agricultural experiments and promotions, agricultural warehouses, various cooperative organizations, civic training, hygiene facilities, and even rural self-defense undertakings. For example, Zouping and Dingxian even use the entire county administration as an experiment in mass education. In terms of undertakings, it already includes countless sciences and is not limited to education. However, in terms of academics, any research must prioritize division of labor and specialized study. Even taking agriculture as an example, those conducting research include the Central Agricultural Experiment Institute and the agricultural colleges of universities. Based on the equipment and talents of mass education institutions, it is feared that they only have the strength to conduct small-scale regional experiments and promotions. The same is true for finance, cooperation, autonomy, and self-defense. The improvement of an entire area requires the entire political and economic structure, which cannot ultimately be solely undertaken by an educational institution. In terms of mass education institutions, how to base their own academic fields, concentrate all their energies and financial resources, and engage in further, narrower, and more controlled experiments; on the one hand, to obtain contact with other institutions and avoid duplication; on the other hand, to gradually standardize effective methods for education and provide them for promotion in various places; to make industries refined through division and efforts substantial through focus is indeed a problem that urgently needs careful consideration. This is especially what I would like to discuss with those responsible for mass education experiments.

Zhu Mao Again Fled to the Border of Sichuan and Yunnan; Bandits Have Fled to Various Roads of the Chishui River and are Being Pursued; Xiao He Suffered Thousands of Casualties, Yongshun Can be Recovered Soon

(Changsha) The chairman of Guizhou, Wang Jialie, telegraphed that Zhu Mao's bandit troops have suffered heavy losses and been severely damaged due to the pursuit by our large army along multiple routes. Unable to gain a foothold after fleeing to western Guizhou, they are rapidly fleeing towards the border of Sichuan and Yunnan provinces. The vanguard of the bandits has reached the Chishui River. Our troops under Wu Qigwei, Zhou Hunyuan, He Zhizhong, etc., are pursuing and blocking the main force of the bandits. The Sichuan army is also launching a fierce attack in the Xugu area. The rearguard of the bandits in places such as Bailakan, Changgan Mountain, Juma Stone, etc., has been repeatedly intercepted by our army, with thousands of casualties and many captives. The bandits under Xiao He in western Hunan have been severely suppressed by our large army and are fleeing in disarray towards Yongshun. Currently, the bandits in Yongxi, Langtou River, Yaping, Shuilongping, and Yongjing Yanxipu, etc., have been repeatedly defeated by our army, and the recovery of Yongshun City will not be difficult. He Jian telegraphed from Chenzhou that the bandits under He and Xiao near Yongshun have been besieged and suppressed by our divisions under Li Jue, Tao Guang, and Zhang Liangji, with many bandits killed. The remnants plan to flee to the border of Hubei, and the recovery of Sangzhi County City is imminent. (Central News Agency, 20th)

Remnant Bandits in Jiangxi and Fujian Are Surrendering with Their Weapons

(Nanchang) Since the ringleaders Fang Zhimin and others were captured by Zhao Guantao's troops, the remnant bandits in eastern Jiangxi have been in a state of leaderlessness. Recently, several cases of surrendering with weapons have occurred every day. Li Desheng, the commander of the pseudo-Northern Fujian Military Region, and Li Zuomin, the pseudo-political commissar, have both surrendered to the headquarters of the Eighth Pacification Zone. (Central News Agency, 20th)

Preliminary Plan for Reorganizing Water Conservancy Agencies: Content

(Nanjing) The preliminary plan for reorganizing various water conservancy agencies by the Water Conservancy Council of the Economic Commission has been submitted to the National Government and approved by the Economic Commission for implementation. The content of the plan includes: (1) The Huai River Conservancy Committee; (2) The Guangdong River Conservancy Committee; (3) The Yellow River Water Conservancy Committee will retain their original names. (4) The Communications Yangtze River Conservancy Association will be renamed the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Committee, with a chairman still appointed by the National Government, and members appointed by the committee. (5) The Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Water Conservancy General Station of the Ministry of Interior will be merged into this committee for handling. (6) The North China Water Conservancy Committee of the Ministry of Interior will be renamed the North China Water Conservancy Committee, with a chairman appointed by the National Government, and members appointed by the Economic Commission. No standing committee members will be established. (7) The organizational method of the Yongding River Conservancy Bureau will be handed over to the Hebei Provincial Government for management. The Yongding River Project Funds Custody Committee will be abolished. If the Hebei Provincial Government deems it necessary, it can be reorganized separately by the Hebei Province. (8) The Taihu Lake Basin Water Conservancy Committee of the Ministry of Interior will be renamed the Taihu Lake Water Conservancy Committee, with a chairman appointed by the National Government, and members appointed by the Economic Commission. Standing committee members will be established separately. (9) The Henan Post-Disaster Relief Project Office will retain its original name and will be jointly operated by the Economic Commission and Hebei Province. All directors and deputy directors will be re-appointed by both the Commission and the Provincial Government. (Special Dispatch, 21st)

Flandin and Simon Express Views Openly; France and Italy Protest German Refusal; The Three-Country Conference is the Most Important in Fifty Years; The League of Nations Administrative Council Sets a Meeting for Early Next Month

The note was two pages long and worded strongly, recognizing Hitler's abandonment of the treaty as illegal. Shortly after, the Italian Ambassador Saluti also submitted a note from the Italian government to Foreign Minister Neuart at 1:00 PM. Although its contents have not yet been disclosed, informed sources in diplomatic circles say that the Italian note is generally the same as the French note, but its wording is more moderate. It is also reported that the German Foreign Minister replied at the time that since other countries do not implement disarmament, the military clauses of the treaty have long been abolished, and Germany cannot accept the protest. Berlin opinion now believes that France will use the three-country conference of England, Italy, and France to be convened in Paris on Saturday to form a line to surround Germany. The House of Representatives has voted three times to trust the government on France's plan to extend military service, and the Senate also passed it yesterday, so the Prime Minister can actually freely dispose of Germany. The French government has stated that it does not fully agree with the British Foreign Minister Simon and Seal Keeper Eden's visit to Germany. Originally, France very much wanted Germany to participate in the British-French Air Force Agreement and allow Germany to restore its military strength after returning to the League of Nations. However, Hitler decided to abandon the treaty without waiting for British diplomats to go to Germany, and France's feelings have changed because of this. Therefore, the notes sent to Germany and the League of Nations today are contrary to British advice. France believes that the diplomatic period is over. The Prime Minister also said in a speech in the Senate that the French army must increase its strength, and France cannot accept Germany's unilateral abandonment of the treaty without consulting with the relevant countries. The Senate has approved the Foreign Minister to go to Moscow to discuss the situation with Soviet Russia. According to unofficial news, Mussolini believes that the Allied countries during the European War should still have a common front for this crisis. (National Telegram, 21st)

French Telegram to Geneva: Requesting a Special Meeting of the League of Nations, Germans Believe it Will Only Increase Disputes

(Paris) France's communication to the League of Nations has been sent today. It is said that this communication does not request an immediate meeting of the Administrative Council, as France believes there is no immediate danger. However, it asks the League of Nations to pay attention to Germany's arbitrary behavior and the damage that Germany's actions will cause to mutual national trust and world peace. League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol will forward the French communication to the President and other council members to decide when to hold a meeting. A meeting can only be convened after a unanimous decision of the Administrative Council. The French press welcomes the resolution of the three countries, England, France, and Italy, to meet in Paris before British Foreign Secretary Simon visits Germany, saying that the cooperation of the three countries is now strong and effective. Berlin has criticized France's appeal to the League of Nations, with much sarcasm. The Deutsche Tageszeitung stated in today's editorial that France's resumption of its alliance policy has long denied the purpose of the League of Nations, and that no matter what action Geneva takes, the progress of this matter will not be affected in the slightest. According to a Reuters dispatch from London, Simon will reportedly propose naval issues during his visit to Berlin. (Reuters, 21st)

(Paris) The French government has recently sent a document to League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol, requesting the convening of the Administrative Council to deal with the problem of Germany's violation of the Treaty of Versailles. The French government's document is recorded as follows:

"On March 16, the German government notified the diplomatic representatives of France, England, Italy, and Poland stationed in Germany, and on the same day promulgated a law stating that the German government has decided to restore compulsory conscription and reorganize the German army into twelve corps, namely thirty-six divisions. Several days before this event, the German authorities openly announced the establishment of an air force. Article 11, paragraph 2 of the Covenant of the League of Nations states that any member of the League of Nations has the right to bring to the attention of the Administrative Council any situation that arises that is likely to affect international relations, thereby disturbing peace or endangering the good understanding on which international peace depends. The situation created by the aforementioned decision of the German government is the same as that stipulated in paragraph 2 of Article 2 of the Covenant. Therefore, the French government specifically brings this attitude of the German government to the attention of the Administrative Council. It would be a great honor, and the problems caused by the aforementioned decision of the German government are extremely important, so I specifically request that an extraordinary meeting of the Administrative Council be convened to review the French government's request. Signed, Laval." (Havas, 21st)

(London) The British political circles regard France's resolution to appeal to the League of Nations as a kind of psychological consolation. However, London is gradually feeling that recent events are very serious and will sooner or later have to be mentioned in Geneva. If an appeal is made to the League of Nations in the future, it does not seem likely that the military provisions of the Treaty of Versailles, which Germany is currently violating, will be cited, nor will Article 16 of the Covenant of the League of Nations on the implementation of economic sanctions be invoked. (Reuters, 21st)

French and Italian Representations to Germany: Differing Content, Not Recognizing Unilateral Treaty Abrogation, German Foreign Minister Rejects

(Berlin) French Ambassador to Germany, Poncet, recently presented a note from the French government to German Foreign Minister Neurath. The note stated: "The French Ambassador to Germany received a notification from the German Foreign Ministry on March 16, stating that the German government promulgated a law on Saturday, deciding to restore compulsory conscription and increase the army's troop strength to thirty-six divisions. A week before this, the German authorities had formally announced the establishment of the German Air Force. The above resolutions are in absolute violation of Germany's treaty obligations and are contrary to the declaration participated in by the German government on December 11, 1932. In that declaration, the German government had promised that the general armament system, which allows Germany and other countries to enjoy equal rights, could not be implemented until a security system was established in various countries. Therefore, the French government is justified in lodging a formal protest against this measure by Germany and, from now on, making various reservations. The French government has always adopted a cooperative attitude and made unremitting efforts to enable Germany to fully participate in the European security organization with great sincerity and consideration for German dignity. Now that Germany has taken this action to violate the treaty, causing anxiety throughout the world, the obligations borne by the countries concerned have been increased, and the German government must bear the responsibility for all the consequences. The French government has decided to seek all means to promote international cooperation in order to eliminate this anxiety and to safeguard European peace. It is hereby reiterated that France has always respected and believed in treaties. Unilateral decisions that undermine international constraints should be rejected from consideration in any negotiations," etc. According to Havas, Foreign Minister Neurath said when receiving the French Ambassador that he had received this protest. In addition, he said that Germany's position was very different from this. (Havas, 21st)

(Berlin) The Italian government sent a protest note to the Italian Ambassador to Germany, Cerruti, for delivery to the German government. The note began by stating, "The Franco-Italian Rome Agreement of January 7 and the Anglo-French London Agreement of February 3 both stated that the main principles of Part V of the Treaty of Versailles concerning the military system cannot be unilaterally changed. Italy maintains that the German armament issue should be discussed in the general negotiations on the issue. This is the same as the Geneva Declaration in which Germany participated on December 11, 1932. The German government also accepted this approach in its notes to England and France on February 14, 1935. Therefore, the Italian government believes that it is justified in making special reservations regarding this decision by Germany and its possible developments." The conclusion stated, "The Italian government believes that the fait accompli created by unilaterally deciding to cancel international constraints cannot be accepted in future talks," etc. (Havas, 21st)

(Berlin) A semi-official German news agency recently released a message stating that after Foreign Minister Neurath received the protest note from the Italian government, he told Italian Ambassador to Germany Cerruti that the reasons on which Italy's communication was based should be rejected, because the other signatories of the Treaty of Versailles had not fulfilled their promises regarding the clauses on disarmament, and they had not adhered to the Treaty of Versailles. (Havas, 21st)

French Premier's Declaration on Germany in the Senate: No Anxiety in Germany Upon Hearing It

(Paris) Today, the Senate convened to discuss the question raised by Senator Le Merit, asking the government by what means it would make up for the shortage of new recruits caused by the decline in population births during the war. Premier Flandin delivered a lengthy speech in response. Finally, the Senate passed a vote of confidence in the government with 263 votes to 21. Flandin's speech first stated that the bill to extend military service passed by the Chamber of Deputies would extend the service period for new recruits enlisting in April 1935 to eighteen months, and the service period for new recruits enlisting thereafter would be extended to two years. He said that this measure was only to supplement the military strength stipulated in the conscription law of 1928 and was not intended to expand armaments. Then, regarding Germany's rearmament, Flandin said, "Shall we tolerate Germany's rearmament? Shall we tolerate the bankruptcy of the disarmament conference? If this is tolerable, what is not tolerable? It is well known that France has always strived to implement disarmament under the conditions of mutual security guarantees. Now, people are unaware and think that Germany's declaration of the abolition of the military clauses of the treaty is a response to the British White Paper and France's extension of military service. They do not know that the establishment of the twelve corps of the German army has been nearly a year, and now it is only formally announced. If this announcement by Germany is accepted by the world, then all peace undertakings based on the League of Nations will be destroyed without exception. As far as we French are concerned, we will never allow Germany to accept this approach. For fifteen years, the French government has spared no effort to promote the cooperation of the two major nations of France and Germany, but the result has been the opposite. France is willing to compromise with Germany, but it is not within the power of France to compromise by despising the truth and denying legal justice. The world will have its own assessment of who is bearing the cost of inciting war. The trust and cooperation between the French and German peoples is indeed what we hope for, but it is futile to talk about trust and cooperation if we abandon our due responsibilities. Furthermore, some people say that France has not fulfilled its obligations to reduce armaments, so Germany has had to rearm. This statement is even more inaccurate. Has the world forgotten that France's standing army has been reduced by 50% since the war? Has the world also forgotten that France's military service period has been reduced from three years to one year? It should be known that France has always looked forward to disarmament like a severe drought looking for rain clouds. The reason why France cannot further reduce its armaments is simply because Germany is rearming. Some people believe that Germany has already fulfilled its obligations under the Treaty of Versailles. This is also definitely not the truth. Germany has superficially reduced its armaments, but in fact, it has been rearming at all times. The world knows that Germany is secretly expanding its armaments, but Germany does not want to admit it publicly. As for France's abandonment of several major clauses of the Treaty of Versailles over the years, what more needs to be said? Unfortunately, Germany has forgotten them all. Today, if people must distort historical facts to prove their sincere desire for cooperation, they can only see that their efforts are becoming increasingly exhausted. Moreover, which country is Germany threatened by that it must rearm? France requests the League of Nations to deal with this serious action, not for the benefit of France itself, but for the common benefit of all countries. World peace is based on justice. Without justice, peace cannot be guaranteed. Therefore, what we are worried about is no longer the problem between France and Germany, but the problem of collective peace. France has sufficient strength to defend its country and to meet the needs of its allies. In addition, there is no shortage of small and weak countries in Europe. If we sit idly by and allow power to replace public reason without taking remedial action, then these small and weak countries will definitely not have a chance to survive. Modifying treaties within the scope of equality among countries is not impossible. France abhors war. We will adopt all measures necessary to maintain peace. From now on, all of us French people should unite with the sacred concept of patriotism, because military preparation and spiritual preparation cannot be separated. Germany's spiritual preparation is an example. Those who oppose the army and the country should be regarded as treason. If propaganda is carried out in the colonies to make the people oppose France, it will be even more intolerable to us. Let us quickly arouse the spirit of patriotism, gather the strength of spirit and matter, and dedicate ourselves to peace, so that the whole world will know that France is united and cannot be easily humiliated. This is what we earnestly hope for," etc. (Havas, 20th)

(Berlin) Officials here have no anxiety over French Premier Flandin's major attack on Germany in the Senate, because his wording is completely emotional. Moreover, up to now, we only know the summary of the French Premier's speech and have not seen the whole picture, so it inevitably increases its threatening tone. (National Telegraph, 21st)

Analysis of the Opinions of the Three British Parties on Germany: The Conservative Party Has Doubts

(London) Regarding Germany's declaration of rearmament and the British government's note to Germany, a debate will be held in the House of Commons today. According to information obtained by Havas, the Conservative, Liberal, and Labour parties will all agree with the section in the government's note to Germany regarding Germany's abolition of the military clauses of the Treaty of Versailles. However, the Conservative Party still has doubts about Germany. The leader of the anti-government faction of the party, former Foreign Secretary Chamberlain, originally wanted to criticize the government for not consulting with France and Italy before deciding to send Foreign Secretary Simon to Germany. However, after hearing that representatives from England, France, and Italy will hold a meeting in Paris this Saturday, the Conservative Party's opposition faction was very satisfied. Therefore, Chamberlain has decided not to criticize the government again. The attitude of the Liberal Party's opposition faction can be seen in the opinion of its leader, Sir Samuel. The party was quite worried when it heard that Germany had restored compulsory military service. Later, because Germany responded to the British note and agreed that British cabinet members would visit Germany, the Liberal Party's opposition faction was very satisfied. Therefore, it will agree with the government's note to Germany. What the party is most concerned about now is whether England, France, and Italy can form a united front at the Paris meeting. As for the Labour Party's opposition faction, its leader, Lansbury, will speak. The party is satisfied with the government's note to Germany, but still has doubts about several points: (1) Whether England, France, and Italy can unite at the Paris meeting; (2) Whether the government will give greater consideration to respecting international treaties than to the actual situation; (3) Whether the procedures set out in the Anglo-French Declaration will be restricted, thereby reducing the possibility of concluding an agreement, so that the various issues inherited from the European War cannot be resolved. (Havas, 21st)

Roosevelt May Also Protest Against Germany: Cautious Due to Domestic Politics

(Washington) Regarding Germany's rearmament, President Roosevelt tends to protest to Germany. The President believes that this expression may avoid or delay the severity of the European situation. However, Roosevelt must be very cautious about this move due to domestic political constraints. Roosevelt's enemies fear that this move will create a "precedent," causing the United States to be dragged into the vortex of European disputes in the future, and use this to attack the President. Therefore, the general public believes that the President will wait until the European political situation is slightly clearer, especially after the results of British Foreign Secretary Simon's visit to Russia are clear, before taking appropriate action. (Havas, 21st)

(Washington) Whether the United States can issue a protest against Germany's violation of the Treaty of Versailles is still being debated by the authorities. However, plans to increase the US naval and land forces have been rushed to completion. Naval Affairs Committee Chairman Vinson announced today that he intends to propose to the House of Representatives: (1) Consolidate the bases in the Pacific; (2) Develop a sufficient naval force to provide the United States with the personnel needed to build all ships in accordance with the treaty; (3) Train sufficient aviators to fly the gradually increasing number of aircraft. House Military Committee Chairman Rodgers has asked the House to consider proposals to establish aviation bases in the United States, Alaska, and Panama, and to form a strong army. Experts in the government cannot agree on the issue of Germany's decision to rearm. Several people expressed their opinions in a private capacity, believing that the US government should recognize Germany's actions as dissatisfaction. Diplomatic advisers believe that the United States has reasons for communication, but it is heard that the authorities very much want to stay out of the matter and not get involved in European disputes. The White House is also said to advocate that the United States should not interfere in any overseas entanglements. According to news here today, the United States may not send observers to the meeting of politicians from England, France, and Italy to be held in Paris on Saturday. (Reuters, 20th)

(Washington) International observers here today expect that the demand for the return of pre-war territories will be Germany's second step. Officials believe that the territories abandoned by Germany include the Pacific islands currently under the trusteeship of Japan. If Germany makes this request, it will have a serious dispute with Japan. The diplomatic community deeply believes that the German government is determined to restore its past position, so it may request the return of territories in order to rejoin the League of Nations. Moreover, in Europe, Hitler may request that the method of the Saar region be used in Austria and the Free City of Danzig, that is, to hold a referendum. President Roosevelt is very well informed about the European situation. In his conversation with the press, he said that the United States will not send a note to Germany, and believes that in the current situation, the United States' "Good Neighbor Policy" may become an important component of the world disarmament movement. The President finally stated that the disarmament movement in Geneva has made great progress, and hopes that the League of Nations can have definite achievements in this matter. (National Telegraph, 20th)

German Defense Minister States: Restore Pre-War Military Strength, Tell the People to Prepare for National Affairs

(Berlin) Defense Minister General von Blomberg published an article in the Vossische Zeitung today, outlining the path that Germany will take to vigorously implement conscription in the future. Since the German government issued an important declaration last Saturday, millions of people have been asking each other about this matter. Blomberg stated, "In the future, Germany's universal compulsory military service will be implemented in accordance with the principles of the National Socialist state." The so-called implementation in accordance with the principles of the National Socialist state means that the national defense organization will restore the original system before the war, because the vision of the National Socialist state is to permanently move forward and never look back. Therefore, people who have received higher education will not be able to shorten their military service as before, only character and achievement can determine the career and value of each individual. The detailed explanation has been fully described in the book "German Military Career". Blomberg also said that since national defense is a major event in which all people participate, there is no doubt that the future will be strong and united. In the future, the potential strength and thoughts in the minds of the people will tend to be consistent and closely integrated. Therefore, the effectiveness of national defense strength is in the present, but it is preparing for the future achievements of the country. (National Telegraph, 20th)

German Espionage Work: National Socialists Mixed into Various Swedish Parties

Stockholm, Sweden - The authorities recently conducted a major search in the Gothenburg branch of the Swedish National Socialist Party, which was set up by workers. According to the documents and letters seized, it is known that the National Socialist Party set up this branch to engage in secret espionage work to undermine enemy parties. According to the description in the documents, it can be seen that there are National Socialist Party members mixed in among the various parties, and their secret work is to list the names of the enemy party members of the National Socialist Party and compile them into a "blacklist". Furthermore, the correspondence between the branch and the German National Socialist Workers' Organization proves that the German National Socialist Party once instructed the Swedish National Socialist Party to carry out political espionage missions for the German National Socialist Party. (Havas, 20th)

Lord Lytton on Russian, Japanese, and German Relations: Emphasizing the Importance of Soviet Russia Joining the League of Nations

(London) Former Director of the League of Nations Far East Incident Investigation Team, Lord Lytton, told a reporter for Pravda, "Cooperation to seek peace cannot be achieved without the participation of the Soviet Union. Therefore, I believe that the Soviet Union's accession to the League of Nations is an extremely important event. At the same time, we must not forget that it is extremely valuable for the Soviet Union to be able to cooperate in the Disarmament Conference. It is extremely clear that the Soviet Union has no plans to invade neighboring countries. The words of politicians in Japan and Germany clearly show that Japan intends to expand westward, while Germany is eyeing the east. They are moving forward to your country. I strongly disapprove of this anti-Soviet alliance between Japan and Germany. Litvinov once said that peace is indivisible, and at the same time, today's wars cannot be limited to local events. I fully agree with this point." Lord Lytton also expressed his support for the establishment of an effective security organization. He particularly supported the Eastern Mutual European Convention, because if this move can be realized, it will be a major victory for the guarantee of peace. (TASS, 20th)

Berlin Air Defense Drill: People's Discipline Strict, Calm

(Berlin) The air defense drill began last night and continued this morning. Residents strictly adhered to the orders issued by the Aviation Ministry. The strict discipline was truly impressive, and it is believable that in the event of real danger, the people will obey the authorities and remain calm. During this morning's drill, enemy aircraft were simulated attacking, with thick black, red, and blue smoke representing bomb explosions, burning houses, and suffocating gas. Upon hearing the alarm, residents immediately stopped their daily activities and rushed to the cellars, with police guarding the entrances to prevent anyone from going out. The drill lasted more than six hours before it ended. (March 20th, Havas dispatch)

American-Russian Relations

(Washington) Since the failure of the US-Russian debt negotiations, some in the United States have launched a movement to sever relations with Russia. Both the Senate and the House of Representatives have proposed bills to cut off relations with Russia. The State Department does not approve of this action, arguing that this is a matter within the President's purview. If these bills are passed, US-Russian relations will be hampered. However, the initiators of the bill have ignored this. Secretary of State Hull stated today that the United States will continue to recognize the Soviet Union. The US Ambassador to Russia, Bullitt, is currently on leave in the United States and will return to Moscow next week to resume his duties. It is expected that Bullitt will reopen debt negotiations upon his return to Russia, but whether he has special instructions is currently unknown. (March 21st, Reuters dispatch)

Soviet Aviation Industry

(Moscow dispatch from TASS, February 26th) Before 1928, the Soviet Union relied heavily on foreign countries for aviation equipment. However, today, all civilian and military aircraft used in the Soviet Union are domestically produced. At the same time, there has been great progress in manufacturing styles. There are three aviation research institutes engaged in this research, with the Moscow Central Aerodynamic Institute being the most prominent. A flying boat manufacturing plant was established in 1931, and the first batch of five experimental flying boats manufactured there range in volume from 2,150 cubic meters to 6,800 cubic meters. Soviet civil aviation is developing rapidly, so the training of pilots and technicians is also essential. The Soviet Union currently has several aviation schools that train various flight personnel. The general public's interest in aviation is growing daily. The most widespread organization is the "Society of Friends of Aviation," with millions of members. The public enthusiastically donates to aviation construction. Interest in aircraft research at high altitudes is growing. In 1933, there was the famous flight of the Soviet Union's "Winged Sphere" balloon, followed by the "Society of Friends of Aviation" balloon in 1934. The Soviet Union's operating air routes will expand to 85,000 kilometers by 1937 (compared to 37,000 kilometers in 1933), and local air routes will increase to 35,000 kilometers (compared to 14,000 kilometers in 1933). The volume of airmail and passenger traffic will increase by 10 to 35 times compared to 1933.

Hitler's Special Envoy Did Not Go to England

(Berlin) Rumors circulated that Hitler's special envoy on disarmament issues, Ribbentrop, would go to London today to meet with British Foreign Secretary Simon and Liberal Party leader Lord Lothian. However, Ribbentrop's staff claimed to know nothing about this, saying that he is currently touring southern Germany and that there is no political reason for him to go to England. (March 20th, Havas dispatch)

Deputy Director of Accounting of the Chinese Eastern Railway Commits Suicide Rather Than Return Home

(Harbin) Savloff, the Deputy Director of Accounting in the General Affairs Department of the Chinese Eastern Railway, committed suicide with a handgun at his residence today because he did not want to return home in a few days. However, as he was an extreme left-wing communist, it is believed that there must be complex circumstances involved. (March 21st, Telecom dispatch)

United States Sells Gold

(New York) Since the United States nationalized all gold held domestically, it has announced the sale of gold for the first time today. The Treasury Department will sell 32,000 ounces of gold to the Bank of Mexico in order to help Mexico maintain its currency reserve. The selling price is three dollars and fifty cents per ounce, which is the legal price. (March 20th, Reuters dispatch)

International Commercial Telecommunications

March 21st, Reuters Special Commercial Dispatch

Gold and Silver

London gold prices fell by one shilling, eight and a half pence yesterday, seeming to have fallen too sharply. Today, with the pound sterling weak, gold prices have recovered, reaching one hundred and forty-six shillings, ten and a half pence, an increase of one shilling, four and a half pence from yesterday.

The London silver market has also shown improvement. Prices fell yesterday but rebounded today. Spot prices are twenty-seven pence, one eight seven five, up 〇 point 〇 six two five; futures prices are twenty-seven pence, three one two five, up point one two five. There were few sellers, and purchases from China were the reason for the price increase, as well as the weak pound sterling.

Exchange Rates

The London foreign exchange market was panicky this morning, with frequent price fluctuations, but not very drastic. Trading volume was low. The opening exchange rate for the US dollar against the British pound was four dollars, seventy-six cents, two five, lower by six two five than the closing rate for the US dollar against the British pound yesterday. After a slight increase, prices mostly declined before noon. The price at 2:00 PM was four dollars, seventy-four cents, nine three seven five, lower by one cent, three two two five than the opening price.

The opening price for the British pound against the French franc was seventy-two francs, one eight, lower by three pounds and eleven pence than yesterday. Prices recovered slightly at 11:00 AM, then declined again. The price at 1:00 PM was seventy-one francs, eight four. At 2:00 PM, it rose by ten pounds to seventy-one francs, nine four, which was still lower by twenty-four pounds than the opening price this morning.

In the New York foreign exchange market, the opening exchange rate for the US dollar against the British pound was four dollars, seventy-six cents, one two five, lower by seven five than yesterday. The French franc rose by two five, reaching six dollars, fifty-nine and a half cents. There was a considerable atmosphere of panic in the market, as the turmoil in Europe caused instability for the British pound and gold coins. The British pound fell to four dollars, seventy-six cents shortly afterward. Market prices remained stable within an hour of the opening.

Cotton and Wheat

New York: Secretary of Agriculture Wallace announced that the government's cotton production policy remains unchanged. This statement should be beneficial to the multi-party. However, the cotton market did not receive a good influence today. The uncertainty of the European situation and foreign sales are the two major factors for the poor performance of the cotton market. Although the opening price rose several points, it soon fell below yesterday's closing price. Fortunately, most of the sales were absorbed, so prices could be maintained. Foreign operators then bought in slightly, and prices rose slightly. In addition, a lot of industry insiders were buying.

Chicago: There were reports of dust storms again affecting Chicago wheat today, and there is a possibility of poor harvests. Therefore, although the Department of Agriculture canceled the restrictions on spring wheat this year, the opening price was still stable. Winnipeg rose point one two five because of the weak pound sterling and slightly higher prices in Liverpool. There were some purchases in the Chicago wheat market before noon, but they were mostly speculative.

Liverpool Wheat: Although there was disturbing news in the United States about the cancellation of spring wheat restrictions, there was still a lot of trading in the Liverpool wheat market today, and prices rose slightly. At 1:00 PM, the price for the May contract was five shillings, one and a half pence, up half a penny from yesterday.

Liverpool Cotton: Because of good sentiment today, there were still many buyers, so prices also rose. At 1:00 PM, the price for the May contract was six pence, one two, higher by eight points than yesterday's closing price.

Rubber

London: The market situation was light today. At noon, the trading price for the July and September contracts was five pence, six two five, lower by point one two five than yesterday's closing price.

New York: Today's forward contracts fell by ten points, and then fell by another ten points in less than half an hour. This is because although the British pound has a weak trend, the London rubber market price has fallen instead.

Securities

New York: Trading was inactive at the opening today, with the situation as it was yesterday. Prices mostly trended downward, and sentiment showed no improvement. The unsettled situation in Europe continues to have a restrictive impact on the market here. The New York stock market prices are listed on the left:

Roosevelt to Approve Philippine Constitution Tomorrow; After Acceptance by the People of the Philippines and Elections, a Republican Government will be Formed Recognizing US Sovereignty

(Washington) President Roosevelt will approve the Philippine Constitution on Saturday, which is the first step towards the complete independence of the Philippines within ten or twelve years. Philippine Senate representatives Quezon and others will attend the grand ceremony for the approval of the constitution. After the Philippine General Assembly accepts this constitution and elections are held, the Philippines will organize a republican government, with the date set for December 30th. The current Philippine Governor-General will serve as a special envoy to the Philippines for several months. It is noted that this constitution stipulates a republican system for the Philippines and recognizes US sovereignty. Philippine officials must swear allegiance to the United States. (March 21st, Reuters dispatch)

(Washington) The Associated Press learned today that commercial talks between US officials and the Philippine delegation have been temporarily suspended while awaiting the United States to decide on its domestic and foreign commercial policies and clarify the international and Far Eastern situation. One of the most difficult points to resolve is that, although the American people have expressed goodwill towards the Filipinos in economic and political aspects, it is practically impossible for the two governments to jointly decide on the policies to be implemented. The President's Good Neighbor Policy is currently the only policy that the Philippine side agrees to. The United States hopes to maintain friendship with South America, the Far East, and Europe through this policy. Qualified observers here say that the Philippine parliament fears foreign opposition to close commercial understanding between the US and the Philippines, and may not take any action to protect American goods on the island thereafter. (March 20th, National News Agency dispatch)

(Washington) Official circles in Washington continued to study the Philippine issue today. The House Committee on Insular Affairs, chaired by Congressman Gaviersky, began its work. It is said that the committee will soon hear opinions from all sectors of the Philippines. The Senate passed the first Philippine appropriation bill, of which $255,000 is for the expenses of the US envoy stationed in the Philippines after the establishment of the Philippine Republic. However, the House only passed $165,000, and this matter will be decided by a joint conference of the two houses. Committee member McClark discussed the Philippine issue with President Roosevelt and later declared that he would prepare a report based on the results of his inspection of the Philippines. Governor-General Murphy and Secretary of Agriculture Wallace discussed a plan to use 3.5 million sugar tax dollars to improve Philippine agriculture for a long time and dined with Secretary of State Philip to discuss Far Eastern commercial issues. (March 20th, National News Agency dispatch)

British Railway Expert to Come to Shanghai After Being Hired by Our Government, Departing from Marseilles on April 5th

(London) Railway authority Brigadier General Hammond, hired by the Chinese government, will soon set off for China to investigate the organization of the Chinese railway system and provide consultation. Two Great Western Railway experts will accompany him. Brigadier General Hammond is 54 years old and served in the European War. Later, he served as the chairman of the Allied delegation to Poland. He then investigated railways in Africa, Greece, and British colonies, prepared reports, and served as a railway advisor to the Indian government. (March 21st, Reuters dispatch)

(London) Brigadier General Hammond, who is going to China to study the railway system at the request of the Chinese government, is scheduled to depart from Marseilles on the RMS Rawalpindi on April 5th to Shanghai and then to Nanjing. According to Hammond, who spoke to a Reuters interviewer, he will pay special attention to what characteristics of the Chinese railway need to be resolved after consulting with the Chinese government. He is prepared to fulfill any duty. This trip to China has no military nature. Brigadier General Hammond is a railway authority who is familiar with all aspects of railway management. Therefore, the British government specially recommended him to meet the needs of the Chinese government. (March 21st, Reuters dispatch)

Japanese Ambassador to the United States Speaks on Sino-Japanese Cooperation

(New York) Japanese Ambassador to the United States Saito spoke today at a banquet of the Japan Society, saying that human psychology is gradually leaning towards peace, and the understanding that war is useless and the gradual extension of justice in international events are the reasons for the new concept of mankind. Statues of generals have been replaced by monuments to nameless heroes, and the mantra of "Right or wrong, I love my country" is no longer accepted by those who value self-respect. Peace and war compete with each other, but he has no doubt about the results. Saito then spoke of the situation in the Far East, saying that the time has come for Sino-Japanese cooperation. China and Japan should be close friends, which is in the best interest of both parties. If Japan can help China consolidate its domestic situation, the whole world will benefit from it. Not only will the Chinese people benefit, but also the commercial and financial activities of Europe and the United States in China will be facilitated and encouraged. (March 20th, Reuters dispatch)

Another Incident Occurs in Italian Somaliland, Demanding Compensation from Abyssinia

(Rome) Another incident occurred in Italian Somaliland, worsening the relationship between Italy and Abyssinia. Rome has just received news that a team of armed Abyssinians invaded Italian territory south of the Yabis Qubi River and looted a hundred camels. These people's ambitions are obviously not limited to this area. However, upon seeing the appearance of a detachment of soldiers belonging to the garrison of Italian Somaliland, they hastily retreated, and fired shots at the pursuing detachment during their escape. Fortunately, there were no casualties. Although this incident is not as serious as the previous two conflicts that occurred in Uruel, the Italians are quite indignant. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, upon receiving this news, immediately instructed the Foreign Ministry to demand compensation from the Abyssinian government. (March 21st, Reuters dispatch)

British House of Commons Questions Investigation of the Slave Problem in Hong Kong

(London) At a meeting of the House of Commons today, Labour MP White asked about the scope of the investigation by the Committee on Slavery appointed by the Governor of Hong Kong. Colonial Secretary Lister's answer was the same as that issued on February 13th, that is, the committee's report will be published in a timely manner. Labour MP Wynn suggested that the committee should investigate the inspection and registration system implemented in Hong Kong, and said that if the current inspectors are insufficient, their number should be increased. Lister replied that the committee would have general instructions to investigate not only specific points, but also the entire issue. If the committee believes that the number of inspectors should be increased, it will have the right to request an increase. (March 20th, Reuters dispatch)

Dramatic Climate Changes in Various Places

(Anqing) The climate in Anqing has been warm recently, almost as if spring is moving into summer. On the evening of the 20th, the wind rose and it suddenly became cold. Around 11:00 PM, it rained, mixed with snow pellets. Heavy snow fell at night, reaching an inch. It all disappeared on the morning of the 21st. The air pressure dropped, and the temperature was only 40 degrees, as if it were severe winter. However, overcast skies prevailed, and there was a possibility of continued snow. According to those familiar with agricultural affairs, vegetables and wheat have suffered considerable damage.

(Xi'an) There has been no rain in Shaanxi Province since the beginning of spring, and spring wheat is eagerly awaiting rain. On the morning of the 20th, it rained heavily. However, it suddenly snowed and hailed before noon, and the climate turned cold, which will inevitably have an impact on the fields. (March 20th, Central News Agency dispatch)

(Nanchang) The climate in Nanchang has been warm for nearly half a month, like early summer. On the morning of the 20th, there was a howling wind, followed by heavy rain in the afternoon, the most violent wind and rain in two months. Ships traveling in the river felt greatly threatened. The climate turned cold at night, and it snowed again on the morning of the 21st. People have changed back from silk and linen to fur coats. Because the winter was too warm, spring epidemics are prevalent, and meningitis has been quite rampant recently, spreading very far. The health authorities are planning prevention measures. With this severe cold, the epidemic is expected to be slightly reduced, and it is also very beneficial to agricultural production. (March 21st, Central News Agency dispatch)

(Hangzhou) In Hangzhou, it snowed after 3:00 AM on the morning of the 21st, followed by heavy snow, but it melted as it fell, stopping around 9:00 AM. The weather turned cold, like severe winter. (March 21st, Central News Agency dispatch)

(Changshu) The weather changed dramatically yesterday, and the temperature dropped to 34 degrees. Heavy snow fell at night, and it did not stop until morning. Although it cleared up at noon, the cold remained unabated, and there was still no sign of prolonged clear weather. (March 21st, special dispatch)

Key Resolutions of the Suzhou Business Federation Meeting

(Changzhou) The Suzhou Provincial Business Federation held a meeting at the Changzhou Chamber of Commerce on the afternoon of the 21st. Chairman Yu Xiaochuan and committee members from 16 counties attended. The following key resolutions were made: (1) The Suzhou Province's newly promulgated regulations on house taxes will be compiled by the Federation, incorporating the opinions of various county chambers of commerce, and earnestly submitted for suspension. (2) A request will be submitted to the Ministry of Finance to expedite the promulgation of the new stamp tax law and temporarily suspend inspections until it is published. (3) The oil and sauce business tax rate should remain at the old rate of two per thousand. (4) A memorial service will be initiated for the late Shi Junqing, former chairman of the Wuxian Chamber of Commerce. (21st Dispatch)

Orders

The National Government, on the 21st, issued an order appointing Ye Xuying as a judge of the Supreme Court. This order also stipulated that the regulations concerning the retirement pay of Air Force officers are formulated and promulgated.

Jinan: Ancient Bronze Artifact Discovered

Shaped like a bronze basin, it can emit sound and spray water when rubbed by hand; numerous archaeologists have studied it but cannot explain its principle.

Jinan Dispatch: Shandong is the ancient state of Qi and Lu, the cradle of Chinese culture, and ancient artifacts are frequently discovered. In the spring of the previous year, thirteen Western Zhou bronze artifacts were discovered in Teng County, causing a nationwide sensation. Recently, a Mr. Zhu in this city also possesses an ancient bronze artifact that is quite peculiar. The following describes its appearance, unique features, and origins:

Shape and Peculiarities

The artifact is round, made of yellow bronze, with an ancient and mottled appearance. It is about the size of an ordinary basin, about half a foot tall, with thirteen characters in relief in the style of inscriptions on ancient bronze vessels. After examination, the first character is "Zhou," and the last character is "Bi," while the rest are unrecognizable. It has two ears, and the bottom of the artifact has a circle, with five bars outside the circle, and four bronze fish cast outside the bars. According to the owner, the circle symbolizes the Taiji, the five bars symbolize the Five Elements, the four fish symbolize the Four Symbols, and the two ears symbolize the Two Instruments. Most remarkably, when water is filled in the vessel and the two ears are rubbed with both hands, it emits a buzzing sound, and the water inside bubbles like boiling water. The longer it is rubbed, the louder the sound becomes, and it can be heard with rising and falling tones, like playing a piano. At the same time, the bronze fish inside the vessel spray water from their mouths above the water surface. If rubbed by an energetic and robust person, the water sprays higher, about two feet, from four points, which is quite a spectacle. If rubbed by an old and weak person, the water sprays lower, and the sound is also softer.

Origins of the Artifact

It is said that the artifact was discovered quite early. During the late Qing Dynasty, Zhang Jian (also known as Zhang Ji Zhi) organized an exposition in Beijing, where various strange objects were displayed. This artifact was also displayed in a separate room, and viewers marveled at it but could not understand its principle. The original owner was a military man, and the current owner, Mr. Zhu, was also serving in the military at that time. He took great notice of it. Not long after, the original owner passed away, and his family sold it to Mr. Zhu for two to three thousand yuan. Mr. Zhu cherished it and brought it to Jinan for safekeeping, not showing it to others. When Zhang Zongchang was in Shandong, someone leaked the information to Zhang, who sent someone to suggest offering him a certain position in exchange. Mr. Zhu then took the artifact to Tianjin. Later, Chu Yupu also learned about it and wanted to acquire it, offering Mr. Zhu a position in exchange. Mr. Zhu secretly deposited the artifact in a bank safe and went to Shanghai alone, hiding his name and staying out of sight. Through numerous moves and expenses, he had already spent a considerable amount of money. Recently, Mr. Zhu's finances have become strained, and he intends to sell it.

Verifications from Various Sources

The owner initially thought it was a rare treasure and was unwilling to show it easily, asking for 50,000 yuan. Later, Wang Xiantang, a librarian at the Provincial Library and an archaeologist, determined that it was an artifact from the Song or Yuan Dynasty, at most from the Tang Dynasty, and definitely not from the Three Dynasties, and that the characters were forged by later generations. However, he could not explain the principle behind the spraying water and sound. Because physics and chemistry had not been greatly developed in the Song and Yuan Dynasties, it was impossible to create this object. Previously, Zhang Taiyan had thoroughly researched this artifact in the "Miscellaneous Notes" section of the National Essence Journal he published in Shanghai, but he was unable to make any discoveries or determine its name. Chen Yuan'an, president of Fu Jen Catholic University in Beiping and a renowned expert in archaeology, especially skilled in identifying ancient bronzes, was asked to study it via letter. Chen replied that the spraying water and sound were due to the action of electricity. The bronze material of the artifact must contain a metallic element that transmits electricity very quickly. Human hands have electricity, so rubbing it transmits electricity to the water, causing it to make sound and spray water. However, with the advancement of modern science, no one has yet discovered a metal that transmits electricity so quickly, and it is astonishing that people in the Yuan Dynasty in China invented it. If it is proven to be a bronze artifact from the Three Dynasties, it would be an even rarer treasure, because it would prove that people in China during the Three Dynasties were able to utilize electricity to create this object. Chen also said in his letter that if there are defects on the artifact and red rust is found inside, it can prove that it is a bronze artifact from the Three Dynasties, because if it is not from the Three Dynasties, it will only have green rust and no red rust. The reporter carefully examined the artifact and found a defect about the size of a bean, inside which there was indeed red rust, so it is possible that it is a bronze artifact from the Three Dynasties. In short, whether the artifact is from the Three Dynasties or not, it is certainly an artifact from the Song or Yuan Dynasty. People in China during the Song and Yuan Dynasties were able to discover a metal that transmits electricity the fastest, which has not yet been discovered in the 20th century, and were able to utilize it to create this object, which is of great significance and research value to Chinese culture.

Not One of a Kind

Recently, the Guangzhiyuan, established by foreigners in this city, also purchased a similar object from Henan, but it is slightly smaller. When rubbed by hand, it can also emit sound and spray water, but the sound is softer, and the water sprays lower. Henan is also the birthplace of ancient Chinese culture, so it is evident that this object is an ancient artifact. This is specially recorded to provide for the research of contemporary scientists.

Lichang Shipping Company's Lichang Steamer Runs Aground in Japan Due to Fog

The ship did not sink, and the crew was rescued; it was insured for 50,000 yuan.

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the Lichang Steamer of Lichang Shipping Company, rented to a Japanese company, carrying cargo from Dalian to Moji in Japan, ran aground due to fog in the harbor waters the other day. Efforts are being made to rescue it. The details are as follows:

Rented to a Japanese Company

Yongyuan Shipping Company's ships are the Yongyuan and Shunyuan, and it also acts as an agent for the Lichang and Lishun, for a total of four ships. They specialize in sailing to Shanghai, Dalian, Yantai, and other places. The head office is located in Dalian, and the Shanghai office is located in the Yongfengli Customs Brokerage on Sijing Road. Starting last year, in order to save expenses, the Shanghai office was closed, and the ships sailing to Shanghai were suspended. The Lichang and Lishun were also stopped being agents in the north. The Lichang was rented to a Japanese merchant by the Lichang Shipping Company to sail between Dalian and Moji, mainly for carrying cargo.

Runs Aground Due to Fog

The Lichang Steamer has a gross tonnage of 1,484 tons and a net tonnage of 815 tons. After being rented to a Japanese company, it carried cargo from Dalian to Moji in Japan. On the 20th of this month, at about 1:00 PM, when it reached the waters of Zhigang in Japan, it ran aground due to fog. The Japanese captain immediately sent a wireless call for help and inspected the point of impact. Although it was broken, and seawater was entering, it did not immediately sink because it was sitting on the reef.

Efforts to Rescue

After the Lichang Steamer ran aground, nearby Japanese ships have already provided assistance, and the cargo it was carrying has been unloaded. All the crew members, about thirty in number, except for the Japanese captain, are Chinese and have been rescued. It has been decided to enter the dock for repairs after it is out of danger. The head office of Lichang is located in Qingdao. After receiving the captain's telegram, they immediately telegraphed Japan to arrange for rescue.

Insured for 50,000

A Xin Sheng News Agency reporter learned from the China Ship Insurance Federation yesterday morning that the steamer had taken out a 50,000 yuan safety insurance policy with the Federation. However, after the ship ran aground, as of yesterday, the Lichang Company had not yet reported it. The Federation has decided to immediately telegraph the Lichang Company in Qingdao to inquire about the details of the grounding so that it can be investigated and processed.

Suzhou: Yao Guangjun, Employee of Shanghai Municipal Bank, Commits Suicide by Drowning

Yao Guangjun, 23 years old, a native of Suzhou and the younger brother of Yao Genghuan, the editor of the Shanghai Minbao's supplement, was an employee of the Shanghai Municipal Bank. His home in Suzhou was located at No. 87 Jiuxueqian. Yao Gengchen, Gengjun's second elder brother, was an employee of the Suzhou Tianye Bank. On the morning of the 8th of this month, Gengjun came to Suzhou from Shanghai and opened room number 39 at the Suzhou Hotel outside Changmen. He wrote a letter to his family in the room, vaguely expressing his intention to commit suicide. It is rumored that the reason was that Gengjun was addicted to dance halls in Shanghai, resulting in financial difficulties that could not be remedied. After his brother received the letter, he published an advertisement in the Suzhou newspaper on the 9th, the original text of which was: "To Fudi, I have read everything in your letter. The matter is still kept secret. I hope you turn back and come home to reunite. There are solutions for everything. From your brother, Xixiang." However, Gengjun went to Tiger Hill from the Suzhou Hotel on the 8th and never returned. Therefore, his family did not receive any further news from him. Until the afternoon of the 21st, Fang Shenzhi, a reporter from the Wuxian Daily, was passing by the Zhenzhuo Bridge on Tiger Hill and glimpsed a floating corpse in the river. Upon closer inspection, it was indeed a corpse, wearing a long gown and trousers, and still holding seven wheat straw fans in his hand. He reported to the police, who retrieved the body, reported to the court for inspection, and conducted an investigation. It was then learned that the deceased was Yao Guangjun. They went to the Suzhou Hotel to inquire and found a small package under the pillow on the bed in room number 39. Inside the package was a photo and a suicide note. His family was notified and came to handle everything.

Wuxi: Abnormal Weather, Spring Snow Flies

The weather has been alternately warm and cold in recent days, with high and low temperatures changing from time to time. After the heavy fog the night before, the temperature suddenly rose, but by the morning of yesterday (20th), the temperature suddenly dropped, with a crisp north wind, as if it were the cold air of late winter and early spring. The Fahrenheit thermometer read 45 degrees. Around 11:00 PM, it began to drizzle, followed by snowflakes. By about 1:00 AM this morning, heavy snow was falling, which stopped only at 5:30 AM. The mountains and fields were covered in silver. However, this kind of spring snow is harmful and not beneficial to crops. There are quite a few cases of scarlet fever and meningitis in the city, and they are all being treated in various hospitals. According to doctors, these diseases are entirely caused by abnormal weather.

Six People Drown in Overturned Boat in Taihu Lake

Lishun Mountain Goods Store, located in Nantang, south of Qingming Bridge outside the South Gate, is owned by Chen Yaoshan. It has been in business for many years, and its business has been fairly good. Recently, as spring bamboo shoots came on the market, Chen sent his employees to Zhangzhu in Yixing to purchase a large batch of spring bamboo shoots in order to meet customer needs. They were transported by a large barge to Wuxi. Unexpectedly, fierce winds and waves struck for several days, and the weather suddenly turned cold. When they reached Taihu Lake, they were attacked by wind and waves and capsized. In addition to all the spring bamboo shoots being submerged, six crew members also drowned. Afterwards, someone reported the incident to Lishun Mountain Goods Store by telephone. After receiving the news, the store hired another boat yesterday to go to salvage the bodies and handle everything.

However, the couple's relationship has not been good, and quarrels often occur. The other day, Du had another quarrel with his wife and told Wang that he was going to marry another concubine and would no longer come home. Wang heard this and was extremely angry, and she conceived a pessimistic thought. Around 7:00 PM the other night, she secretly swallowed one yuan of raw opium and committed suicide. Huang Ying, a 17-year-old girl from a certain house on Dongpo Road in Hangzhou, recently suffered some kind of stimulation and suddenly conceived a pessimistic thought.
