Local News

Ministry of Finance Issues 100 Million Yuan of Public Bonds to Rescue the Market

Replenishing the funds of the three banks to indirectly aid industry and commerce; the bank subcommittee discussed and decided on credit lending measures yesterday.

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that, regarding the issue of rescuing the market, the Ministry of Finance has decided to issue 100 million yuan of financial public bonds to replenish the funds of the three banks and regulate the market, with industry and commerce credit lending. The bank association subcommittee met yesterday and decided to persuade the Qianye Association to join and raise a syndicate to implement it. The details are as follows:

Issuing Public Bonds to Bolster the Funds of the Three Banks

The Ministry of Finance has decided to issue 100 million yuan of financial public bonds of the Republic of China in 1935 to rescue industry and commerce, secured by customs revenue. It has been approved by the Central Political Council. Of these public bonds, 30 million yuan have been allocated to replenish the funds of the Central Bank, 25 million yuan to replenish the funds of the Bank of China, and 10 million yuan to replenish the funds of the Bank of Communications, so that the funds of the three banks can be increased to strengthen themselves in order to circulate finance and regulate the market. The financial circles in Shanghai have expressed their approval of the Ministry of Finance issuing public bonds to rescue the market and replenish the funds of the three banks. Once implemented, the fear of a shortage of funds in the market can be reduced, so that industry and commerce can gradually restore their original state.

Three Banks Offer Lending to Rescue the Market

The Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, in the final accounts of 1934, designated a huge amount of money to rescue the market, to be used for mortgage lending to the silver and money industries, which is still continuing. However, the total amount is less than 10 million yuan. Now the three banks have decided to further increase the amount of money after the financial public bonds of 100 million yuan are issued, to be used for mortgage lending to the silver and money industries. Although it is directly lending to the silver and money industries, it is indirectly lending to industry and commerce, because after the silver and money industries obtain the money, their own strength will be strengthened, and their ability to lend to industry and commerce will also increase.

Bank Subcommittee Held a Meeting Yesterday

The subcommittee organized by the bankers association on the industrial and commercial credit small loan of 5 million yuan held its first meeting at the association on Hong Kong Road at 2:00 PM yesterday. The attendees were committee members Chen Guangfu, Tang Shoumin, Bei Songsun, Ye Fuxiao, Xu Jiying, Wang Yansong, and six others. Lin Kanghou, the secretary-general of the association, attended as an observer. All the committee members agreed that industrial and commercial credit small loans should be implemented quickly to provide assistance. The following resolutions were made: (1) A letter will be sent to persuade the members of the Qianye Association to continue to increase their lending appropriately to cooperate, otherwise, the member banks will recognize the amount in full. (2) A syndicate of industrial and commercial credit small lenders will be formed immediately, striving to hold it as soon as possible. (3) The procedure is that all applicants must first fill out a three-part application form, send it to the local association and the municipal chamber of commerce for approval, and then send it to the syndicate for review and approval. The designated member bank will then pay the loan. The meeting adjourned at 3:00 PM.

Loan Syndicate is Being Organized

A Xin Sheng News Agency reporter learned from the silver and money industries yesterday that the Qianye Association has decided not to join the syndicate in the industrial and commercial credit small loan case after a temporary meeting of member representatives. They have now advised member banks to expand their lending as much as possible. As for the bank association's resolution to persuade them to join the syndicate, no letter has been received as of last night. After receiving the letter, it will be submitted to the executive committee for discussion. As for the bank association, it has decided to set up the fund with the Central Bank of the government. The total amount is 5 million yuan, with the Central Bank responsible for 2.5 million yuan, and the member banks of the association jointly responsible for 2.5 million yuan. It would be best if the members of the Qianye Association can take part of it.

Implementation of Assistance, Hope for Revival

The local association, the municipal chamber of commerce, etc., have decided on five concrete measures to provide assistance, and they have all been gradually implemented. Regarding cargo mortgages, the silver and money industries have been doing as much as possible. The Central Bank has sent a letter to the municipal chamber of commerce saying that acceptance bill discounting can be done according to the regulations. The industrial and commercial credit loan syndicate has been organized and will be realized soon. Now the Ministry of Finance has decided to issue public bonds to replenish the funds of the three banks and regulate the market. Therefore, after the efforts of all parties, there is no problem regarding rescuing the market. The foreign exchange rate in the money market yesterday has dropped to six points, and there is hope for the revival of industry and commerce.

Pan Yangyao's Remarks

The Decline of Industry and Commerce

The situation is not as bad as rumors suggest; the biggest reasons are no more than three points.

Central News Agency reports that industry and commerce in this city are declining, and appeals have been made to find ways to provide assistance. The Ministry of Finance, for the sake of assistance, has submitted a proposal to the Central Political Council to issue 100 million yuan of financial public bonds. At the same time, the banking circles in this city will also contribute 5 million yuan together with the Ministry of Finance to provide loans for assistance. In order to understand the decline of industry and commerce in this city, a Central News Agency reporter paid a special visit to Pan Yangyao, who is familiar with industry and commerce in this city, yesterday morning. According to Pan's findings, the decline of industry and commerce in this city is not as bad as rumors suggest. The details are as follows:

Decline Situation

According to Pan, in this time of economic downturn, the decline of industry and commerce in this city is to be expected. It is not just industry and commerce that is like this, but all industries are in this state. The decline of industry and commerce is much exaggerated in recent rumors. According to my own investigation, I dare not fully believe the rumors to be true. According to a survey of industry and commerce throughout the city, the recent business situation is that more than 40% are profitable, 30% can obtain official interest, and the rest are losing money. This situation is inconsistent with the rumors. However, if assistance is not provided immediately, the future of industry and commerce will be dire. Therefore, the financial authorities and the financial circles of this city will provide financial assistance in practice.

Biggest Reasons

As for the decline of industry and commerce, although the reasons vary, the most important ones are no more than three points. The first point is meager interest. According to the price statistics of the Jincheng Bank in this city, last year's prices were 10 to 16 percent lower than the previous year. With lower prices, interest is naturally meager. The second point is the accumulation of inventory. In recent years, the purchasing power of the market has been weak, so inventory is piled up like mountains, putting aside part of the cost. After the goods are sold, they are given to the merchants, and the payment cannot be received for a while, which puts aside another part of the cost. At the same time, the purchase of raw materials also puts aside another part of the cost. The third point is competition among the same industry. Recently, competition among the same industry has become increasingly fierce, often causing the selling price to fall below the cost. With industry and commerce in this kind of layer-by-layer suffering, it is declining day by day.

Methods of Assistance

People in industry and commerce have gradually understood this kind of layer-by-layer suffering, and they are now doing their best to find ways to provide assistance. They are even more saddened by the point of competition among the same industry. Therefore, a group of industry and commerce leaders has consulted several times, and they all agree that in order to avoid competition among the same industry, it is necessary to first know the sales and production numbers of the goods in that industry and restrict each other so that the production number is suitable for the sales number, so as to avoid the accumulation of inventory. At the same time, they must unite the ambition of competition among the same industry and compete with foreign goods, so that all malpractices can be avoided.

Loans for Factories

For the sake of their own interests, the silver and money industries must, of course, be careful when lending to industry and commerce, which makes it even more difficult for industry and commerce whose capital turnover is not smooth. Some people in the industry have advocated organizing groups to borrow money from the silver and money industries, but it is difficult to predict when it will be implemented. For example, more than ten factories are united to form a lending group to borrow a certain amount of money from the silver and money industries. If one of the factories in the group goes bankrupt or cannot repay the money, the remaining factories will be jointly responsible for compensating for the debt. In this way, the silver and money industries can lend to industry and commerce with peace of mind, and the industry and commerce economy can also be more flexible.

The Public Works Department Sends Police to Protect the Soviet Russian Consulate to Prevent White Russian Demonstrations

The "North China Daily News" reports that when the Russian ship "Northern" arrived in Shanghai last time, a medical officer had escaped from the ship, and its engineer, Davydov, 24, also went ashore and did not return. Later, he went to the Soviet Russian Consulate once. At the end of the year, he suddenly disappeared. The White Russian expatriates in this port widely rumored that Davydov was being detained in the Soviet Russian Consulate and that his life was in danger. Some people also said that they had seen Davydov in ragged clothes standing in front of the window, looking haggard, through a telescope from a house opposite the Soviet Russian Consulate. Now the "Northern" has sailed to Songkou again, and the White Russian expatriates are afraid that Davydov will be secretly transported back to the country. Therefore, some people are wandering in front of the consulate to spy on it. The Public Works Department's General Police Department sent many police officers to be stationed around the consulate and the Garden Bridge to prevent White Russians from demonstrating in front of the consulate. Those who went to the consulate to inquire were told that the consul general, deputy consul, and other personnel were not in the consulate, so no one was responsible for answering.

Luo Qinghua Advocates Commercial Acceptance Bills, Sends Letters to the Cotton Cloth and Dyeing Industries to Adopt Them Consistently

"New Voice" reports that since the Silk Industry Association created commercial acceptance bills, it has aroused deep attention from all walks of life. Economists Yang Yinpu, Zhang Naiqi, and Zhang Xiaomei have all written articles in favor of it. The Bankers Association has set up a subcommittee to discuss implementation methods. The Sino-British Bank has also agreed to discount bills. The members' congress of the Electrical Machinery Silk Industry Association resolved to proceed in the same way as the silk industry. Luo Qinghua, the supervisory committee member of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the chairman of the Silk Industry Association, has been particularly active in promoting this matter. Yesterday, he sent letters to the cotton cloth industry leader Ke Ganchen and the dyeing industry leader Zhu Wenqi, asking them to adopt this type of bill consistently to remedy the defects of currency contraction. The original letter is recorded below: "Since the continuous outflow of silver from Shanghai since last year, the financial turnover has suddenly felt difficult, and the market panic has become increasingly profound. It has become an undeniable fact that all parties are running around and shouting for help. Examining our country's commercial trade, most of it relies on accounts receivable. For the sake of turnover, industry and commerce have always relied on the credit loans of money shops for support, and the loans obtained are then sold to customers on credit. As a result, what the silver money shops get are the accounts receivable of the industrial and commercial sectors, and what the industrial and commercial sectors get are the accounts receivable of customers. This type of debt cannot be transferred or circulated. As a result, once there is a shortage of funds in the market, they become deadlocked with each other. Most of the panic this time was caused by the outflow of silver, but tracing back to the long-term cause, it cannot be said that it was caused by the imperfect account receivable system. I believe that industry and commerce should have a sense of self-awareness and self-rescue at this time of difficulty. In the past, the Chamber of Commerce and leaders of various industries have met and talked about the fact that accounts receivable make funds lose their flexibility and business is hindered, and they have suffered deeply from this type of account receivable system. Over the years, I have been planning methods for rectification and reform, but because all parties are comfortable with the old ways, there are many obstacles and it is difficult to implement them. As a result of the financial turmoil in the city last winter, I knew that the market would be even more desolate this spring, and the financial industry would mainly tighten loans. After repeated discussions with my colleagues in the industry, I believe that the only way to remedy the currency contraction today and lay the foundation for the future revival of industry and commerce is to create commercial acceptance bills. The reason for this is that this type of bill has been practiced in various countries for a long time, and both buyers and sellers feel it is convenient. The seller has a definite date for receiving the money for the goods, and can also hold it to the silver money shop to discount it. In this way, the currency is increased invisibly, the turnover is flexible, and the business can gradually develop. The buyer pays on time, so there is no lack of preparation. Therefore, since this case was passed by the members' representative congress of the Silk Industry Association, and a letter was sent to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to forward it to various industries for consistent promotion, economic experts such as Zhang Naiqi, Yang Yinpu, and Zhang Xiaomei have all written articles in favor of it, believing that it is worthy of promotion. Qinghua has visited many advanced figures in the financial industry, who also said that this is an urgent plan for today. Recently, the Bankers Association has set up a special committee to discuss discount promotion methods, and the central government has also replied to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce that it will agree to re-discount it. Today, industry and commerce are calling for relief and running around to tell each other that the only thing they say is that there are not enough chips and the turnover is not flexible. If this type of bill can be used universally, and accounts receivable can be turned into bill receivables, then the chips that are increased will be more than 10,000 times. If the silver money shops agree to discount them, but industry and commerce are afraid of reform, stick to the old ways, and procrastinate and delay, then how will they explain themselves? Therefore, the public association and the electrical machinery silk weaving factory industry have decided to consistently use this type of commercial acceptance bill and eliminate the receipt system from April 1, in connection with cotton cloth and other related businesses, which are like lips and teeth. I also hope that Mr. will lead his colleagues, have a vision, and have a plan regarding the use of commercial acceptance. He will definitely be happy to agree. I have presented the experience of creating and attaching a copy of the origin, and I have written a letter asking you to submit it to your association for discussion and implementation, so that we can consistently adopt it, accelerate the circulation, and achieve greater results, which will benefit the country and save the people, and is not shallow.

The Cooperation of Promoting Domestic Sugar Has Been Effective; the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and Others Have Offered Encouraging Words; the Company is Scheduled to Officially Open on the 24th

"New Voice" reports that the Shanghai Sugar Industry Association, in order to promote domestic sugar, has united its member sugar companies and raised 300,000 yuan to organize a sugar industry cooperative limited company. It has submitted an application to the competent authorities for registration in accordance with the Company Law, and undertakes the sale of Guangdong's machine-made sugar. The method of bidding is adopted, which is very fair. After hard work, it has been quite effective. The more than 30,000 bags of Guangdong sugar that have arrived in Shanghai have been sold out. The company is scheduled to hold an opening ceremony on the 24th, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and others have encouraged it. The details are as follows:

Encouragement from the Chamber of Commerce

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce gave words of encouragement for the company's opening, saying that sugar is a necessary food for people's livelihood. Since Taiwan was ceded, the sugarcane production in the inland provinces has become even smaller, and foreign goods have been oversupplied. Sugar has become one of the biggest sources of loss. Recently, Guangdong Province has improved sugarcane varieties and established factories for refining, which will revive the sugar industry and benefit people's livelihood. The Shanghai Sugar Industry Association, all of its members, aware of the importance of promoting domestic sugar, upholding the spirit of mutual assistance between production and sales, and gathering huge amounts of capital to organize a sugar industry cooperative company, are doing their best to promote sales, and can be regarded as those who promote domestic goods and practice what they preach. It is truly a self-awareness of the business community. The long-standing bad habits in our country's business community have been that each person operates for his own private interests and is ignorant of the country's ties, just like the ancients said, "Winning does not give way to each other, and losing does not save each other." As a result, once a foreigner competes, it is like soup pouring into a crucible. Since your company takes cooperation as its symbol, it should pay attention to the meaning of the name, develop mutual assistance and cooperation, and get rid of bad habits. In addition to recommending domestic sugar, it will also be a new atmosphere for the business community. The saying goes, "Praise does not forget the rules." At the beginning of your company's development, I dare to raise this meaning to encourage each other. Sincerely given by the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

Words of Encouragement from the Industry Association

The Sugar Industry Association congratulated the company's opening, saying that our country's sugar-making industry began in the Tang Dynasty, and production became more prosperous by the Ming and Qing Dynasties. More than 60 years ago, not only was it self-sufficient, but it could also export to foreign countries. In modern times, science has prospered, and the sugar of all countries is machine-made. Domestic sugar, on the other hand, sticks to the old methods and does not know how to improve, which has led to the invasion of foreign sugar and filled the market. A few years ago, domestic sugar was almost eliminated, and the amount of loss was as high as 10,000 every year. The money of a country is like the marrow of a person's body. If it often flows out, how can it survive? Therefore, all citizens should rise up to rescue and share the responsibility of blocking the loss. In 1935, the Guangdong Provincial State-run Machine-made Sugarcane Sugar Factory was established, and its products are superior to foreign sugar. They are responsible for production, and we are responsible for sales. They are trying to revive domestic sugar in order to block the loss. Shanghai is an area where foreign sugar is rampant. In order to sell this budding machine-made domestic sugar, it is necessary to make unremitting efforts. Our industry upholds this responsibility and unites to establish a sugar industry cooperative company as a group to promote domestic sugar. At the beginning of the organization, all colleagues graduated together and realized the great righteousness, overcoming difficulties to succeed. We share the difficulties of co-creating and understand the magnitude of the mission we bear. We must sincerely help each other, and use the strength of the group. Those who are in charge should do their best to follow, and those who share their success should especially cooperate to help, so that the people will be united, the name will be true, and the benefit of the country will be good. You can give me thicker encouragement to me. Shanghai City Sugar Industry Association.

Zhabei and Yangjing Districts Schedule Opening of Land Value Tax Collection; Collection Scheduled to Begin on April 1 and End on May 31

The Municipal Finance Bureau issued a notice yesterday: "It has been investigated that the first installment of the provisional land value tax for the 24th year should be collected in the following weis (areas) in Zhabei District: Tian Yu Di Zi Yuan Zi Huang Zi of Map 1, Yu Zhou Zhou Zi Hong Zi Huang Zi of Map 2, Ze Zi Chen Zi Su Zi Lie Zi of Map 4, Yuan Zhang Yu Han Zi Lai Zi of Map 5, and Shu Zi Wang Zi Qiu Zi Shou Zi of Map 6; and the following weis in Yangjing District: Ri Zi of Map 2, Zhang Yu Shu Zi of Map 3, Cheng Zi Diao Zi of Map 5, and Zhi Zi Yu Zi Lu Zi Jie Zi Wei Zi Shuang Zi Jin Zi of Map 6. Collection is scheduled to begin on April 1 of this year and end within two months on May 31 of this year. Those whose land is in Zhabei District should bring their previous receipts and pay at the Municipal North Tax Collection Office of this Bureau on Datong Road in Zhabei. Those whose land is in Yangjing District should bring their previous receipts and pay at the Municipal East Tax Collection Office of this Bureau at Chunjiang Wharf in Pudong. Those who fail to pay within the deadline will be summoned and pursued in accordance with Article 8 of the Provisional Land Value Tax Regulations and Article 23 of the Implementing Rules. Annual interest will be added to the amount owed, and the income from the land will be extracted and auctioned for compensation according to the length of the arrears in order to comply with the regulations and prioritize tax collection. In addition to reporting to the Municipal Government and sending out notices, this notice is hereby issued to urge taxpayers to abide by it and pay within the deadline, without any delay, so as to avoid punishment. Those who have not yet received the notice should, within the deadline, provide the map wei number and qiu (area) of the land location and their current residential address or mailing address to the bureau for clarification and supplementary issuance of the duplicate. Meanwhile, they should still pay based on the previous receipt without delay. This notice."

Shanghai Telephone Company Plans New Billing Method Again; Tiered Increase Unfavorable to Merchants; All Industries Continue to Oppose Resolutely

According to the New Voice News Agency, after the Shanghai Telephone Company applied to the two Municipal Councils to increase telephone charges, it has been resolutely opposed by Chinese and foreign people. The Municipal Council has not yet approved it. The company has changed its plan and applied again for implementation. This time, the new telephone rate adopts a usage-based system, which is slightly different from the previous rate requested. The details are as follows: (1) The minimum usage per month is 100 calls, with a charge of 10 yuan. (2) For 101 to 200 calls, each call costs an additional 5 fen. (3) For 201 to 300 calls, each call costs an additional 4 fen. (4) For over 300 calls, each call costs an additional 3 fen. According to this method, 1,000 calls per month would cost a total of 45 or 46 yuan, and over 130 yuan for three months. Therefore, the company has changed the previous method of collecting fees once every three months to collecting fees monthly. However, this method is even more unfavorable to merchants than the previously announced rate. Therefore, all industries are currently opposing it.

Roads Slippery; Fire Truck Overturns; All Injured Sent to Guangci Hospital

Hongtaixiang South Goods Store, located at No. 255 Zhaozhou Road, Xilin Road, West Gate, Nanshi, is opened by Zhu Ruiqing from Jiading. It has been operating for three years. At 2:30 AM yesterday, the store suddenly caught fire. The nearby police officer discovered it and immediately reported it to the Fire Brigade by telephone. The Fire Brigade immediately sent a fire truck to extinguish the fire. Nearby stores were awakened from their sleep and scattered in all directions, causing extreme chaos. The fire was completely extinguished around 4 AM. However, when the fire alarm was sounded, it happened to face the Municipal Council building at No. 117 Lanweiai Road in the French Concession. Therefore, the French Concession Fire Brigade also drove to assist. Unexpectedly, the No. 7 fire truck of the Baojian Road Fire Brigade, led by Frenchman Pelan Sitaro and nine firefighters, driven by driver Li Dexing, drove straight east. Unfortunately, it was raining heavily at the time, and the road was extremely slippery. Therefore, the truck lost its balance. When it reached the corner of Jin Shenfu Road and Lafayette Road, the driver accidentally turned the steering wheel, and the front of the truck rushed straight onto the sidewalk on the right, breaking two sections of a large tree on the roadside. The truck was bounced back by the tree, and the body of the truck overturned, also knocking down the second, larger tree. As a result, all the people on the truck fell under the truck. Driver Li Dexing bore the brunt and was the most seriously injured. The firefighters Yuan Changhai, Sun Jiyi, and Xie Youfu were also seriously injured. Frenchman Pelan Sitaro's eyes were scratched by broken glass from the front of the truck. Shao Aqiu, Liu Wanzi, Zhao Jinhai, and Xia Baogen were slightly injured. The French police heard the news and immediately called an ambulance to the scene. The injured people were carried onto the car one by one and sent to Guangci Hospital for treatment. It is reported that none of the injuries are serious. The damaged No. 7 vehicle has been towed back to the Fire Brigade for repair.

Chongming County Detains Dalian Steamer; For Smuggling Opium

The Yongyu Company's Dalian steamer is a direct Shanghai-Chongming liner, making a round trip every day, coming to Shanghai from Chongming in the morning and returning to Chongming from Shanghai in the afternoon. In January of this year, Da Shu You arrived in Chongming from Shanghai. When it arrived at the port, it was routinely inspected. At that time, the police of the County Public Security Bureau found 1,000 packages of opium smuggled from Shanghai to Chongming in the Dalian steamer's accounting room. The narcotics were confiscated. After the large quantity of smuggled opium was discovered on the Dalian steamer, the Chongming County Government investigated the case. Since the criminals were not caught on the spot, the crew members were detained for questioning, and the opium was confiscated. The county government lightly fined the shipowner and let the matter drop. Unexpectedly, two months have passed since the incident. It was considered that no more problems would arise. Unexpectedly, recently, the county government received an order from the superiors to investigate the case. The old case was brought up again, and the ship had to be investigated in order to pursue the main criminal of smuggling narcotics. On the 19th of this month, the Dalian steamer sailed from Shanghai to Chongming. After the ship docked at Nanmen Port, the County Public Security Bureau sent police officers on board to summon the ship's accountant to the county office for detention. On the morning of the 20th, the Dalian steamer planned to sail to Shanghai as usual. Before the ship was launched, the County Public Security Bureau received an order to seal and detain the ship. The Da Shu Hao was immediately guarded by police officers and detained in Chongming, not allowed to sail until the case was investigated clearly. The Yongyu Company originally had two ships, the Da Yun and the Dalian. The Da Yun had an accident and sank, leaving only the Da Shu Hao. The general manager is Du Shaoshi. The Dalian steamer is only over 300 tons. After Shanghai received the telegram from Chongming, it had to temporarily suspend the Shanghai-Chongming route of the ship. General Manager Du Shaoshi believes that even if the crew members are suspected, it seems to have nothing to do with the ship itself. Once it is detained, it will hinder transportation. Therefore, he is already trying to request the Chongming County Government to release the ship.

Taihu Civilian Boat Robbed

Bandits Abduct Two Women; Boatman Shot and Wounded

Hao Ruyun from Chaohu has a civilian boat with a load of over 1,500 dan. His family members were also on the boat, along with a total of more than ten hired boatmen. He used to specialize in transporting porcelain from Jiangxi to Shanghai, unloading it to earn a living. Recently, the transportation of porcelain has been slow, so he changed to transporting miscellaneous grains and other goods. He recently loaded 1,500 bags of wheat purchased by a Shanghai flour mill in Jingjiang. He immediately sailed to Shanghai. Hao felt that traveling on the outer river was a long journey, so he traveled on the inland waterway to Shanghai, which could save several days of travel and arrive in Shanghai earlier to deliver the goods. When sailing to the Taihu County river area on the border of Jiangsu and Anhui, west of Changzhou, and sailing fast with the wind, five or six small boats suddenly sailed towards them. They were carrying a large group of lake bandits, who fired several shots into the sky and ordered them to stop. Hao saw this and immediately told the helmsman to turn the rudder and sail back. The bandits noticed this and fired at Hao's boat, chasing after them. However, the bandits' boats were smaller and faster, and they were eventually caught. At that time, two boatmen had already been shot and were lying on the deck. About forty or fifty bandits from the small boats, carrying guns, rushed onto the boat and asked the boatmen who the owner was. Hao was hiding in the back cabin and was pointed out by the crew. The bandits entered the cabin, dragged Hao out and beat him. Hao's wife was holding a child, and Hao's two younger sisters were also in the back cabin. When the bandits saw them, they immediately started to molest them. Two bandits who looked like bandit leaders told Hao's wife and sisters not to be afraid and to come out of the cabin quickly. Hao's wife and sisters cried and refused to come out of the cabin. The two bandit leaders ordered the bandits to drag them out, and they dragged Hao's wife and two sisters away, boarding three small boats separately and sailing west first. They searched all the cabins, robbing over 100 yuan, two suitcases, and other stolen goods, and sailed away on the small boats. After the bandits left, Hao saw that his wife and two sisters had been abducted and was very anxious. Suddenly, his wife returned to the boat on a small boat. The bandits released her because she was too old. He did not know where his two sisters had been taken. Hao had no choice but to set sail. Because the boat was damaged, he stopped in Kunshan. Yesterday, Hao came to Shanghai to report to the Shanghai Flour Mill, begging for help to rescue his two sisters.

Financial Gamblers Captured at New Asia Hotel; Punished Separately Yesterday Morning

Huafu Deputy Detective Xue Zhimin and Huatan Yang Dechun of the Old Zha police station learned the night before last that someone was gathering to gamble in room 68, 6th floor of the New Asia Hotel on Nanjing Road. Men and women were mixed together, and there were many people, making profits by taking commissions. They secretly went to the address and arrested the owners Pan Agang, Wang Ruihai, and Wang Qiansheng, and 39 gamblers including Li Shouzhong, Zhu Aling, Zhu Tangshi, and Du Wangshi. The gambling equipment pai gow, 224 yuan in cash, 124 double-jiao coins, chips, dice, etc. were confiscated and taken to the police station separately for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the criminal court of the First Special Court. Zhang Shizhu, the police station's lawyer, filed a lawsuit according to law. Judge Ye interrogated them one by one and clearly sentenced Fan Agang to two months in prison, Wang Ruihai to one month in prison, Wang Qiansheng to a fine of 60 yuan, and the rest to a fine of 30 yuan. The gambling equipment and money were confiscated. Kang Xinxiang and Zhang Weiqing, two of the gamblers, were detained for a later hearing next Monday.

Conspiracy to Bomb Cargo Ship to Obtain Insurance Money; Case Concluded

Ouyang Tai Returned to Custody; Chen Zheng Paid Original Bail; Court Ordered Sentencing on the Morning of the 27th

The Shunan Company's Shunan steamer sailed from Shanghai to Fujian and other places on September 13th last year. When the ship arrived in Sanduwo, Fujian, the shipowner Ouyang Tai went to the customs office there to surrender, pointing out that the company's manager Chen Youbai instructed him to destroy the ship and cargo to claim insurance money. The Lun (court) ordered that Ou and the ship be detained together. The company's chairman, Zheng Zhongwu, sued the local court and detained Chen Youbai for sending to the court. The police were also sent to the Minhou Local Court in Fujian to transfer Ou to Shanghai. Zhang Zi, the prosecutor, repeatedly interrogated Zheng Akang, Zheng Zhongwu's brother, and determined that Chen Youbai, Ouyang Tai, and Zheng Akang were endangering public safety and should be prosecuted. Details have been reported in previous newspapers. The details of the prosecution and the opening of the trial are recorded below. The criminal facts are briefly stated as follows: Chen Youbai is the manager of the Shunan Steamer Company, and Ouyang Tai is the shipowner. On that day, the ship sailed from Shanghai with over 300 tons of goods, a total of 13,467 pieces, to Xinghua. Chen Youbai planned to sail the ship to the shallow waters outside Xinghua and set it on fire. In advance, he falsely reported to the customs that there were over 700 tons of goods, a total of 29,722 pieces, secretly insured it, and planned to claim compensation. On the evening of the 12th of the same month, he invited Ouyang Tai to the Yangzi Hotel, and after discussion, he gave him three bottles of igniters and a forged insurance policy from the Tianxiang Company in Beihai for 4,800 yuan as a reward. He also instructed Zheng Akang, the brother of the company's chairman, Zheng Zhongwu, to act accordingly. When the ship arrived in Xinghua, Ouyang Tai was afraid of harming the lives of the passengers and could not bear to implement the plan. He announced it to the public and sailed to the Sanduwo Customs Office to surrender. He planned to send a telegram to the company but was stopped by Zheng Atai. After the incident, Zheng Zhongwu filed a complaint. The reasons for the prosecution and the legal provisions violated: Although Chen Youbai denied the above facts, Ouyang Tai confessed how Chen Youbai came up with the idea, how he instructed him to discuss it at the Yangzi Hotel, and how he gave him three bottles of igniters and a 4,800 yuan insurance policy as a reward, and instructed him to set the fire outside Xinghua. He clearly confessed everything. Chen Youbai also admitted that he falsely reported over 700 tons of customs goods. According to the letter from the Jianghai Customs Supervisory Office, the Tianxiang Company insurance policy for 4,800 yuan was also denied by Mao Yifa, an employee of the Tianxiang Company. There is no doubt that Chen Youbai secretly forged it. Zheng Akang knew the situation and participated in the preparation. According to the unanimous confessions of the ship's crew members Lin Senfan, Lin Hongchou, Wang Juxing, and Sheng Fuchen in the First Brigade of the Fujian Provincial Water Police, Zheng Akang fled as soon as he arrived in Fujian, which shows that he was guilty. Therefore, Chen Youbai, Ouyang Tai, and Zheng Akang are suspected of committing the crime in Item 4 of Article 187 of the Criminal Law. The plaintiff, Zheng Zhongwu, hired lawyer Lu Dingming and requested a civil lawsuit, requesting that the defendants Chen Youbai and Ouyang Tai jointly compensate the Shunan Steamer Company for 55,000 yuan. Liu Enrong, the criminal court judge, opened the trial several times without a conclusion. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Liu opened the third court again for a continued trial. On the plaintiff's side, the private prosecutor's agent, lawyer Lu Dingming, appeared in court. The defendants also hired lawyers Xue Jiaqi and Zhuang Dingxun to appear in court to defend them. After the judge took the seat, he ordered the detained Ouyang Tai and summoned Chen Youbai, Zheng Akang, and others to the case for questioning one by one. The judge concluded that the case was clear and invited Prosecutor Zhang Zui to the court to present his opinions. The lawyers on each side began their debate for a long time. The judge deemed the trial concluded and scheduled the sentencing for 10:00 AM on the 27th of this month. Ouyang Tai was returned to custody. Chen Youbai and Zheng Akang were still released on their original bail.

Robbery at Chongrang Li, Fuzhou Road; Jiachang and Tongshun Companies Lose Thousands of Gold

At around 5:45 PM yesterday, four or five robbers suddenly arrived at Jiachang Silk Store and Tongshun Cotton Cloth Store at No. 8 Chongrang Li, Fuzhou Road. Three of the robbers, all dressed in long robes, were armed with pistols. They broke into the stores and guarded all the shop assistants and employees, forbidding them from making any noise. The remaining robbers were stationed at the door and in the alley to keep watch. At that time, the shop assistants, seeing that the robbers were armed with weapons, were all terrified and unable to resist, allowing the robbers to do whatever they wanted. They were forced to hand over the keys to the silver cabinets. As a result, the important silver cabinets of both stores were opened, and the robbers were able to search and loot as they pleased. After about half an hour, they finally escaped after plundering. When the shop assistants regained their composure and stepped out to chase, the robbers had already disappeared. The losses of the two stores were checked and amounted to over a thousand gold. They immediately reported to the Central Police Station, requesting a search.

Approximately 70,000 Pills in Total; Li Degui Arrested in Suzhou

At 6:05 PM on the day before yesterday (the 20th), the 80th passenger train departed from the North Station, bound for Wuxi. A freight car was added at the end of the train to carry packages for delivery to Xuzhou. Yao Jianlan, a package driver, and two packers, Li Degui and Chu Yushan, accompanied the car. At about 9:40 PM, when the train arrived at Suzhou Station, Li jumped off, carrying 15 packages of red pills (approximately 70,000 pills), all bearing the Five Continents Divine Horse brand, into the car, intending to transport them elsewhere for sale. The scene was witnessed by a police officer who boarded the train to inspect it and discovered a large amount of drugs. The officer immediately detained the person and the goods and took them to the police station for detention. Li, who claimed to be a 44-year-old from Anhui, was escorted to Shanghai the next morning for further investigation. Yao Jianlan, the package driver, and Chu Yushan, the other packer, were allowed to travel west with the train due to a lack of evidence. It is reported that when they arrived at Wuxi Station, both of them escaped without a trace.

Dragon Shun Shipyard Owner Huang Youbin Accused of Abandonment

Nearing Sixty Years Old, Yet Surrounded by Concubines

Plaintiff Was Initially a Servant, Later Taken as a Concubine

Huang Youbin of Ningbo, who established the Dragon Shun Shipyard in Longhua and prospered in business, accumulating vast wealth and living comfortably, despite being nearly sixty years old, his romantic nature remains undiminished. A woman named Huang Zhou, filed a lawsuit in the local court, accusing Huang Youbin of abandonment and neglect, requesting the recovery of living expenses. Her statement alleges that in 1924, she was seduced by the defendant, Huang Youbin, and has been in such a relationship for ten years, bearing a child. At the child's one-month celebration, Huang Youbin invited relatives and friends to a banquet and named the child Huang Hu, who is now nine years old. Later, they moved to No. 3 Yunheng Lane, Yangchang Lane, outside Xiaonanmen. Initially, the relationship was harmonious, but the defendant's fondness for promiscuity led him to take four concubines after the plaintiff. In September of the year before last, he also took a woman from Suzhou named A Feng and rented a house to live with her. The defendant's heart is devoid of affection, desiring more after obtaining one thing, and becoming weary over time, discarding her like worn-out shoes, and taking new pleasure, living a sweet life, thereafter regarding the plaintiff as a thorn in his side, frequently provoking quarrels and beatings, disregarding the plaintiff's livelihood. She requests a one-time payment of 13,000 yuan for living expenses. After receiving the lawsuit, the court, yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, held a hearing presided over by Judge Yao Fuxiang. The plaintiff, Huang Zhou, testified as above. The defendant, Huang Youbin, testified that he is fifty-six years old, from Ningbo, and vehemently denied the plaintiff's allegations. The judge asked if Xu Helin mediated the matter, resulting in an agreement for you to pay her 20 yuan per month for living expenses. Huang replied that she was slandering him. The judge said that the household registration can prove the facts. Finally, the witness Hu Changfa testified that he is fifty-four years old, from Ningbo, a fruit merchant, and used to be a neighbor of the plaintiff, Huang Zhou. In the summer of 1924, Zhou was introduced by me to work as a servant in Huang's house. Later, I don't know how, Huang married her as a concubine. The judge did not believe it, and ordered the summons of Zhang Yujin, the landlord of No. 2, Wu Jia Lane, Dadongmen, to confront the case, so that the truth could be revealed. The questioning official obtained the testimony and deemed it necessary to summon the witness, ordering a continuation of the interrogation after the witness is summoned.

The Main Culprit Who Killed Yang Jiaxiang, Yang Wenchang, and Others Readily Confess

—The court ordered the conclusion of the debate and scheduled the verdict for the 28th—

Yang Jiaxiang of Haimen, who lived in a flat in the countryside of Li's residence on Julu Dian Road in the French Concession and cultivated a garden, was lured on the evening of February 5th of this year to the barren cemetery at the foot of the Caojia Lane No. 1534, Xiahfei Road, where he was fatally wounded in the head with an axe. The murderer fled, and it was not until the next morning that his fellow villager, Zhang Huojiang, discovered him while passing by and reported it to the French Concession police. Two murder axes were found next to the body, which was taken to the morgue for examination. After examination by the Second Special District Court, it was determined that the body would be collected by the relevant authorities, and the police were ordered to arrest the murderer. It was not until 5:00 PM on the 9th of this month that Bao Zhenglong, a detective from the French Concession police, apprehended the main culprit, Yang Wenchang (27 years old, from the same village and living in the same residence as the deceased, but not of the same clan), and the accomplice, Gui Jinhu (25 years old, from Chongming, also living in the same residence as the deceased), at the intersection of Songshan Road and Datiebang, and escorted them to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and investigation. The details have been recorded in previous reports. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Li Changnian, accompanied by clerk Wang Baoxun, convened the fifth criminal court to continue the trial. Attorney Yuan Jiahuang represented the police department, stating the investigation process of the police department, and prosecuted the two defendants for premeditated murder under Article 284 of the Criminal Code. Yang Wenchang confessed that he and the deceased, Yang Jiaxiang, also known as A Er, lived in the same house and were always on good terms. He wanted to ask me to rob the property of Dr. Li's house on the night of December 29th, but I refused because I was timid. On the night of the 29th, he invited more than ten people to come and forced me to go with them. Because I couldn't refuse, I pretended to agree to go and secretly went to Dr. Li's house to report to the Li family and called the police. I didn't go home that night, but stayed in a small inn in Xieqiao. On the first day of the new year, I went home and heard that the Li family had been robbed the night before, and according to Gui Jinhu, Yang Jiaxiang cursed me behind my back as a "half-devil" and wanted to kill me. I thought that if he wanted to kill me, since he was a robber, I might as well kill him first. So I discussed it with Gui Jinhu. The axe was prepared by Yang Jiaxiang. On the evening of the second day, Gui first took the axe away. At 11 o'clock that night, Gui Jinhu still called Yang Jiaxiang out, walked to Caojia Lane, and killed him. I chopped him once, and he snatched the axe from my hand, causing the handle to break. Gui Jinhu helped chop him once. After the incident, I fled back to Haimen. Recently, I was arrested when I came to Shanghai from my hometown. Gui Jinhu confessed that Yang Jiaxiang said in front of me that Yang Wenchang was a "half-devil" and wanted to kill Wenchang. I advised him that he was his own friend, so he should be lenient. Jiaxiang said he must kill him. So I told Wenchang, and Wenchang wanted to strike first and asked me to help. I agreed. So on the afternoon of the second day of the new year, I took out Jiaxiang's axe and handed it to Wenchang. At 11 o'clock that night, I went to call Jiaxiang and said to him, "Someone is waiting for you outside to talk." He was playing cards and put down the cards and followed me outside. When he walked to Caojia Lane, Wenchang chopped him once first. He snatched Wenchang's axe, and I also chopped him once. I am a middleman, a friend to both sides. Yang Jiaxiang wanted to kill Yang Wenchang and also asked me to help. Yang Wenchang wanted to kill Yang Jiaxiang and also asked me to help. I was in a dilemma and had no way out, so I had to help. At this point in the court interrogation, Li Yusheng (i.e., Dr. Li) and his daughter-in-law, Li Hua, were summoned to the court. They claimed that on the night of the 29th of the old lunar month, more than ten robbers came and robbed them of nearly 40 yuan in cash and three pieces of clothing. They did not report it to the police at the time. They could not clearly identify the faces of the robbers. Then, the police department's lawyer, and the lawyers selected and appointed by the defendants debated each other. After that, the court announced the conclusion of the debate and scheduled the verdict for the 28th. The defendants were still remanded in custody, and the two murder axes were stored in the warehouse.

According to His Confession, He Robbed Because He Had No Other Way to Make a Living

The bandit Xu Defu, 33 years old this year, from Jiangbei, was arrested and sent to court in 1929 for robbery, where he was sentenced to imprisonment. He was arrested by the French Concession police a few days ago. Chen Huazhang, Owner of Sheng Shun Ji Construction Factory, Fined for Obstructing Official Duties

Chen Huazhang, a local, 53 years old this year, the owner of the Sheng Shun Ji Construction Factory at No. 4 Raul Dong Road, French Concession, was sued by a lawyer of the Shanghai Bank in the Civil Court of the Second Special District Court at the end of last year for failing to settle an overdraft of more than 2,000 yuan. When Judge Ma Yishu issued a summons and sent bailiff Wang Shaozu to deliver it, Chen refused to accept the summons and insulted and threatened Wang. He also failed to appear in court on the court date. After the default judgment, on the morning of January 4th of this year at 11:00 AM, Wang Shaozu was again sent with two police officers to deliver the judgment. Chen was lying in bed and became angry when he saw Wang, throwing the judgment on the ground. The men and women in the room surrounded Wang and the police officers and tried to make things difficult for them. Another police officer reported to the police, who sent detectives to resolve the situation. Chen hid during this time. Bailiff Wang and the police officers returned to the court to report to the presiding judge, who transferred the case to the prosecutor's office and sent police to arrest Chen. After opening the court to investigate, it was determined that he had committed the crime of obstructing official duties, and he was ordered to pay a cash bond of 1,000 yuan to await prosecution and trial. Later, the case was concluded by the Preliminary Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court, which sentenced Chen Huazhang to two months of imprisonment. Chen refused to accept the judgment and hired a lawyer to appeal to the Criminal Collegial Panel. The court opened the trial a few days ago, announced the conclusion, and scheduled the date for the verdict. The details have been recorded in the newspaper. Yesterday was the date of the verdict. The appellant and the attorney were not present. Presiding Judge Wang Gangxu and Judges Cao and Liao specially convened the Second Criminal Court to issue a judgment, revoking the original judgment. Chen Huazhang insulted a public official while performing his duties according to law and was fined 300 yuan.

Huang Xiaogang Acts Audaciously and Recklessly, Forging Letters with the Intention of Fraud

Li Xida, a Ningbo native residing at No. 44 Songqing Lane, Qipu Road, his wife Zhao, named Caidi, is from Yixing, 24 years old this year, has a son and a daughter. The son is six years old, and the daughter is only three years old. On January 22nd of this year, around 7:00 or 8:00 PM, she left without saying goodbye due to a minor argument. Although Li searched everywhere, her whereabouts were unknown. He had no choice but to print leaflets and distribute them, offering a reward of 50 yuan to anyone who found her. Until the 15th of this month, Li suddenly received a letter in his wife's name, instructing him to leave 65 yuan in the public reading room of the Feihong Elementary School on Peng Road that afternoon, with the secret mark "One Zero" on the wall, and then come to collect the money. After the money was collected, she would return home. Li suspected a scam, so he reported it to the Huishi Police Department and ordered detectives to go there and act accordingly. They waited all day but did not see anyone come to collect the money. On the 19th, Li received another letter with the same content, still instructing him to carry out the same method on the afternoon of the 20th. Li reported it to the Huishi Police Department again, and Chinese detective Xie Zhiguang handled it according to law. At 3:20 PM, a Cantonese man named Huang Xiaogang came to read the newspaper and soon took the money. The detective stepped forward to arrest him and took him back to the police station. When questioned about the whereabouts of Li's wife, Huang confessed that he did not know where Li's wife was. The two letters Li received were actually written by me, hoping to defraud him of 65 yuan. He was escorted to the Fifth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court yesterday morning. Judge Huang Risheng opened the court for interrogation. Police lawyer Jiang Baolian stated the previous situation and prosecuted him according to Article 363 of the Criminal Code, requesting punishment. Huang Xiaogang confessed that he forged the plaintiff's wife's letter with the intention of fraud. Judge Huang reviewed the confession and ordered Huang to be remanded in custody, scheduling the verdict to be announced on the morning of the 23rd.

Lu Genquan and Tan Yuan Settle Their Lawsuit

Lu Genquan, the owner of Lu Gen Ji Construction Factory, previously hired Lawyer Jiang Chiping to sue Tan Yuan, the engineer of Hengyao Construction Company on North Suzhou Road, in the First Special District Court for defamation, etc. The reason for the lawsuit was that Lu contracted the Jin family's house on Jiangwan Zhengde Road, which caused a dispute over the water connection problem of the Zhabei Water and Electricity Plant, leading to the lawsuit. Tan also filed a counterclaim. The result of the first trial was that both parties were declared not guilty. Both parties expressed dissatisfaction with the judgment and filed an appeal to the Collegial Panel. Presiding Judge Qian Hongye had summoned them for trial once and advised them to try to settle the matter because it was a minor matter. Therefore, during this postponement, close friends intervened to mediate, and both parties, adhering to the judge's earnest advice, dispelled their misunderstandings and did not want to continue the lawsuit for a long time. Therefore, the lawyers of both parties submitted petitions yesterday to request the withdrawal of the appeal. Presiding Judge Qian approved it, so the case came to an end.

Li Yuding Carries a Fake Pistol to Rob

Li Yuding, a laborer, colluded with Li Xiaorong and Chen Yunhua, who are still at large, on the afternoon of the 8th of this month, at around 7:00 PM, carrying a fake pistol, to rob the property of Chen Chonglin, a Ningbo native, at No. 719 Dongyouheng Road. However, the woman, Ge Mei, was vigilant and frantically sounded the police whistle on the upstairs window. The gang panicked and fled, and the next day, they mailed a threatening letter, demanding 5,000 yuan and instructing someone to contact them near Maojia Stone Bridge in Hongzhen, otherwise, there would be a threat to their lives. The Huishan Police Department was notified. Detective Pi Bingzhang and detective Shen Binkui of the Red Chinese Squad arrested Li Yuding on the morning of the 12th at the Yong'an Hotel, No. 4, Lane 598, Tangshan Road, and escorted him to the First Special District Court. He denied the threatening letter part. He was ordered to be detained for further investigation. Yesterday morning, Judge Jiang Shuzi came to the Third Criminal Court for investigation. Lawyer Ru Baoyi of the Public Works Department stated that after checking the handwriting of the defendant during the postponement, it did not match the threatening letter and was irrelevant. When questioned, the defendant confessed that when they went to rob, Li Xiaorong was the mastermind, and the fake gun was also given by him, instructing him to go inside first to check the situation. Unexpectedly, the upstairs pulled the echo (i.e., blew the police whistle). I fled in panic. I don't know who wrote the threatening letter. Please investigate. Judge Jiang ordered him to be remanded in custody and scheduled the verdict to be announced.

Chen Genbao Arrested for Selling Red Pills

Chen Gengshi, a Ningbo native, was found carrying a can of the drug "red pills," totaling 240 pills, on his person at 4:15 PM the day before yesterday while passing through Huade Road. Chinese detective Ji Peijin saw that his appearance was suspicious and intercepted him, finding the drug pills. Upon questioning, he learned that he had bought them from Kou Er, a Qingjiang native at No. 4, Lane 112, East Xihuade Road, for two yuan. He rushed to arrest him, but was unable to find him. Chen was taken to the Huishan Police Department, and the police chief ordered him to be detained. Yesterday, he was escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District. Lawyer Ru of the Public Works Department stated the previous situation and filed a public prosecution according to Article 6 of the Anti-Smoking Law, requesting a strict punishment. Then, Detective Ji reported the matter again and presented a large can of drug pills for inspection. When questioned, the defendant confessed that he sold them for profit. Judge Jiang ordered him to be remanded in custody and scheduled the verdict to be announced.

The Municipal Government Provides Relief to Rickshaw Pullers

The Social Affairs Bureau Drafts a Plan Outline

The rickshaw pullers of this city are suffering greatly due to the economic downturn and the pressure of life. The municipal government is paying close attention and has specially asked the Social Affairs Bureau to draft an outline of the city's relief plan for rickshaw pullers and submit it to the municipal government for approval and implementation. We will specially explore and record its outline as follows: (A) Start-up methods: 1. Conduct rickshaw puller registration; 2. Relief for surplus rickshaw pullers; (B) Fundamental methods: 1. Construct labor new villages; 2. Hold cooperative education, health, infant care, insurance, and other welfare undertakings; 3. Public rickshaws; (C) Transitional methods: 1. Labor tea gardens; (D) Work allocation: 1. Conduct rickshaw puller registration and public rickshaws, which will be handled by the municipal government; 2. The remaining work will be handled by another rickshaw puller welfare association. The organizational members of the welfare association are divided into the following types: (1) Basic members: rickshaw pullers; (2) Supporting members: enthusiastic people and groups; (E) Funding planning: 1. Return part or all of the rickshaw donation as funding for the construction of the new village; 2. The city government has recently designated 500,000 yuan in loans to provide relief to rickshaw pullers. Please use this amount as the starting funding for public rickshaws; 3. The membership fees paid by the rickshaw pullers will be used entirely for relief and for holding welfare undertakings for rickshaw pullers (except for the new village); 4. The supporting members' membership fees will be used as salaries for the welfare association staff and office expenses.

The Chamber of Commerce Cables the Ministry of Finance, Requesting Correction of the Stamp Duty Dispute on Return Slips

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce cabled the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing yesterday, stating, "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, on the 20th of this month, according to a letter from the Shanghai Biscuit, Candy, and Canned Food Industry Association, member Yan Shirong, the manager of Xinghua Chocolate Candy Factory, came to the association with an invoice and a goods return slip from the factory, stating that after our factory completes a transaction with a customer, we instruct the deliveryman to send it, with an invoice and return slip as proof of receipt for both parties. The invoice is stamped as usual, but after reviewing the Stamp Duty Law, there seems to be no explicit provision for stamping the return slip again, so it is no longer stamped. Unexpectedly, the stamp duty inspectors recently took away dozens of pages of return slips, and they will definitely impose arbitrary fines, requesting relief, etc. Based on this, after checking, the invoice has already been stamped as usual, so there is no need to stamp the return slip again. In order to obtain a basis for this, we have specially attached a copy of the invoice and the return slip and request your association to quickly study them and provide instructions on whether the Ministry of Finance requires return slips to be stamped, so that we can forward them for compliance." Two sample slips were attached to the association. After checking the factory's invoice, it is divided into two slips, one given to the customer for storage and one given to the customer to stamp and returned to the factory for storage. Its nature belongs to a type of delivery return slip. In other words, it is a goods receipt. According to the current Provisional Regulations on Stamp Duty, only cash receipts are stamped, and there are no goods receipts that are stamped. Since the factory has stamped the main invoice, the other slip used as a return slip should not be stamped according to regulations. The inspectors may have misunderstood the law and are deliberately demanding it. It is appropriate to send the same type of slips for your Ministry to examine and approve, and to issue a general order to correct the situation, so that merchants and inspectors can follow it. It is truly for the public convenience. Sincerely, Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

Hua Aman, a 23-year-old man from Suzhou, had been unemployed for a long time and felt overwhelmed by economic pressure. He suddenly had suicidal thoughts. Yesterday at noon, he went alone to the Haijing Road pier and jumped into the Huangpu River to kill himself. Fortunately, he was rescued by a boatman and sent to the public security water police station. After learning about his plight, they deemed him pitiable and ordered someone to find his younger brother, Quan Gen, to take him home.

Also, Liu Yueyun, a 22-year-old man from Guangdong, could not find employment in Shanghai and lacked the means to survive. Yesterday at 1 PM, he jumped into the Huangpu River at the Taikoo Dock in the French Concession to kill himself. He was spotted by a Chinese detective from the customs water police station, who quickly devised a way to rescue him and brought him to the police station. After some words of encouragement from the Chinese officer, he was ordered to find his friend, Liu Zhuming, to take him home together.

Inspection Report of the Central Bank

227th Time

The 227th inspection report on the issuance reserve of the Central Bank states: In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve for the exchangeable banknotes issued by the bank. The 227th inspection was conducted at the bank's issuing bureau on March 20, 1935. The results of the inspection are hereby announced as follows: (A) Total amount of exchangeable banknotes issued: 88,519,409 silver dollars, including 81,669,135 silver dollar notes and 6,850,274 subsidiary currency notes. Total amount of exchangeable banknote reserve: 88,519,409 silver dollars, including 69,456,201.22 silver dollars in cash reserve. This cash reserve includes 65,693,698.22 silver dollars stored in the bank's issuing vault, 1,953,910 silver dollars stored in branches in various ports, and 1,808,591 silver dollars deposited with other banks. The security reserve is equivalent to 19,063,207.78 silver dollars. (B) Total amount of Customs Gold Unit exchangeable banknotes issued: 373,324.70 Customs Gold Units. Total amount of Customs Gold Unit exchangeable banknote reserve: 373,324.70 Customs Gold Units. This reserve includes 7,351.95 taels of silver, valued at 5,0779, equivalent to 373,324.70 Customs Gold Units. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank Exchangeable Banknote Regulations, the cash reserve should be 60% and the security reserve should be 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60%, and the security reserve is less than 40%, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is hereby submitted. March 21, 1935, Li Fusun, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank; Supervisors Xie Mingxun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, and Xu Jiying.

Longhua Temple's New Look

With the arrival of spring, there are many visitors to Longhua, either to worship and offer incense at Longhua Temple or to admire the scenic spots inside the temple. This is the peak season for tourists. Moreover, the temple is undergoing extensive construction. Not only have the Buddha statues in the halls been newly decorated, but also the collapsed beams and broken pillars of the past are being carefully repaired to restore the temple to its former glory. The abbot of the temple, Xingkong, has recently stipulated that all pilgrims who donate more than one yuan must be issued a receipt to prevent abuse. Recently, the monks of the temple also held a notification ceremony to warn against wrongdoing. The text of the ceremony states: "All monasteries in the ten directions are without appearance or sect, universal in Tao, and impartial. Fearing internal and external misunderstandings, and that our painstaking efforts may not be understood, we hereby follow the Baizhang Pure Rules and strictly announce this warning. I, Abbot Xingkong, am ashamed to be in charge of Longhua, but as the ancients said, 'If the monastery is not well managed, the Dharma wheel will not turn.' Those who harm the monastery or encroach upon its assets will lose their blessings, have their lifespans shortened, suffer from terrible illnesses, or encounter disasters. At the end of their lives, they will fall into the three evil paths and all evil realms. May the gods witness this and serve as a warning to those who come after."

Water Thief Xue Wenhua Captured

Xue Wenhua, also known as Yao Kui, a water thief, lives in Sanwanchang, Lujiazui, Pudong. He used to be a "Taili Ren" (cargo inspector) at Jardine Matheson & Co., but had been unemployed for a long time. He relied on wearing a tin pen on his ear and carrying a ledger to pose as a cargo inspector and sneak onto various ships to steal goods for a living. Yesterday morning, he went to the Qichang Warehouse pier in Pudong as usual, and stole a clock of considerable value from the foreign Banhuowen merchant ship. He hid it on his person as he disembarked, but his clothes bulged, and he was spotted by a Chinese detective from the Customs Water Police Station. He was arrested along with the stolen goods and taken to the police station. Under strict questioning, he confessed to repeatedly stealing typewriters, telescopes, gold watches, and other items from various ships. The police chief immediately ordered him to be sent to the local court in the afternoon for interrogation.

Qingda Industrial Cooperative Produces High-Quality Sealing Wax

Qingda Industrial Cooperative, located at 1455 Jing'an Temple Road, was founded since the central government designated this year as the National Goods Year. They are deeply concerned about the increasing imports of foreign goods and the outflow of money. The amount of sealing wax lost each year is also alarming. Record of the Wuxi Fellow Villagers Association Meeting

The Wuxi Fellow Villagers Association in Shanghai convened a general membership meeting on March 3rd and voted to elect the third session of directors and councilors. As a result, seventeen people, including Kuang Zhongmou, were elected as directors, and fifty-one people, including Ren Nongxuan, were elected as councilors. Subsequently, problems arose with this election, so a joint meeting of the old directors was specially convened yesterday to discuss the matter. Those present included Tao Renqian, Kuang Zhongmou, Sun Qiuping, Liang Xieyong, Xiao Xiaoren, Qin Gangsun, Cha Zhongkang, Rong Ruichang, You Rongbo, Shi Fuhou, Wang Yaochen, Gu Zhizhong, Jia Chunhua, Chen Shuan, Pu Zhida, Zhao Xianji, Xu Keting, Sun Zhidao, and Zhu Junsheng, among others. Kuang Zhongmou chaired the meeting, and Xiao Xiaoren took the minutes. Matters for discussion: Yao Zhongkang, Rong Ruichang, Liang Xieyong, Qin Gangsun, and Pu Zhida proposed that since non-members participated in this election, the ballots should be opened and reviewed first. If any violations are found, it would be appropriate to re-vote and re-elect. Xu Keting, Wang Yaochen, Shi Fuhou, Zhao Xianji, and Gu Zhizhong all seconded the proposal. However, Chairman Kuang believed that since Feng Xuchen and Liu Xinquan, who handled the sealing of the ballots, were not present, it was not convenient to open them, and he refused to do so. He immediately left the meeting to express his firm stance. After some persuasion, it was resolved to appoint Jia Chunhua, Xiao Xiaoren, Sun Qiuping, and Zhao Xianji to communicate with both sides and seek a compromise. However, the majority opinion was that the matter should be handled in accordance with the law, and the ballots should be reviewed first. If they are legal, the new officials should take office immediately; otherwise, a new vote should be held to ensure prudence.

Calligraphy and Painting News

Exhibition of Paintings by Li Zhurui Li Zhurui from Shaoxing is skilled in painting, especially landscapes. In the late Qing Dynasty, he worked in Sichuan, and later settled in Chengdu, using painting to express himself. Now over seventy years old, his achievements are rarely seen in the world. His landscapes are majestic and possess all six principles of painting. Xu Beihong once inscribed one of his paintings, saying, "The wrinkles and dots are ancient and simple, yet the sight is fresh and novel. There are no such figures in the north and south of the Yangtze River today." Huang Binhong also praised him as "proficient in all six principles, unparalleled in the contemporary era. It is a pity that he lives in seclusion in Sichuan and is therefore rarely seen by the world." Recently, because of the Red Bandit invasion of Sichuan, Li has come to Shanghai to avoid the chaos. Friends have advised him to make himself known to the world. However, Mr. Li believes that he is too old, and Shanghai is only a temporary residence. He still plans to return to Sichuan soon. Recently, the Baowenzhai Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition in Beijing opened, and friends begged him to display several of his works, such as "Scenes of Mount Emei," "Realistic Sketches of the Three Gorges," and "Kuanglu Peaks," all of which are masterpieces. Mr. Li resides at 48 Yongyu Lane, Ximen Road, Shanghai. Art lovers should consider it an honor to see his work.

Relocation of Painter Tang Dongfu Tang Dongfu has long been famous for his paintings. His landscapes inherit the family learning of his ancestor, Duke Zhenmin, and his brushstrokes are detached and unrestrained, very different from contemporary styles. He has recently moved to 6, Lane 5, Fanshe Lane, Moore Road. Major stationery and fan shops have his price list and accept painting commissions on his behalf. These few words are recorded to inform those seeking Mr. Tang's paintings.

Letters to the Editor

Dear Editor, I have read in your newspaper today about the lawsuit filed by Ms. Lu Ping against the Tongchang Motor Company for defamation, which involves me and is inconsistent with the facts. I have checked and found that I did not receive a subpoena from the court beforehand, which is why I did not appear in court. I did not refuse to appear. Furthermore, I have been the director of the Tongchang Advertising Department for many years and have a deep relationship with the company's young owner. Last year, due to the economic downturn, my salary was high, and although the young owner did not say so explicitly, he often looked troubled. At that time, I had many other jobs, so I offered my resignation, and Chu Liangfang, a returned student, took over the position. The statement that the business has been suspended concerns my reputation. I request that you make a correction immediately. I am grateful for your assistance. Sincerely, Mao Keming. March 21st.

Dear Editor, I recently read in your newspaper on the 9th about the news of the establishment of the Shanghai New Anhui Fellow Villagers Association, in which my name was listed among the attendees. I am currently staying at the school and have not left my house. It is obvious that someone else fabricated this. I am writing to request that you publish a correction. Thank you for your cooperation. Wang Kaimin. March 20th.

Special Announcement

Jin Cheng Bank's Business Report for 1934 (9)

(1) The Soviet Union's Second Five-Year Plan for production places special emphasis on the electrification of industry and the collectivization of agriculture, aiming to become a country that equally values agriculture and industry. Therefore, since its implementation, both agricultural and industrial production in the country have developed rapidly. For example, the production of grains (including rye, wheat, barley, and oats) was estimated at 58.5 million pounds in 1932, but increased sharply to 75.1 million pounds in 1933, and further increased to 80.1 million pounds in 1934. In terms of industrial production in 1934, coal production was 92 million tons, an increase of 21.4% compared to 75.8 million tons in 1933, and an increase of 126% compared to the production in 1929. Petroleum production was 25.6 million tons, an increase of 19.6% compared to 21.4 million tons in 1933, and an increase of 76.6% compared to 1929. The value of machinery production increased by 22.5% compared to 1933 and more than quadrupled compared to 1929. Electricity production increased by 29.3% compared to 1933 and more than tripled compared to 1929. Pig iron production increased by 46.4% compared to 1933, steel production increased by 39.6% compared to 1933, rolled steel production increased by 43.4% compared to 1933, superphosphate fertilizer production increased by 30.8% compared to 1933, automobile production increased by 4.0% compared to 1933 and more than septupled compared to 1929, and tractor production increased by 28.11% compared to 1933. Looking at the overall index of industrial production (1929 equals 100), there has also been an increase in recent years, with the index being 130 in 1930, rising to 162 in 1932, 185 in 1933, and further rising to 239 in 1934.
